##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-11 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq DRB to slice association (ID: 11144140)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-11.0-4**  (ID: `11144169`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq [Before CB008828-C]

For all structures within drbAddReqPs list field of PsUser_UserSetupReq message (received from CP-RT) L2-PS shall store information about DRB to slice association (snssai structure) if available, regardless of slice awareness has been configured or not for both configured and unconfigured slices (For further details refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17581_replaced([11188712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvd22_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_11072_replaced([11176812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_262zyfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If DRB is associated to the slice that don’t exist on configured or unconfigured slice list, L2PS should add that slice to the list of unconfigured slices.

This information is needed in case slice aware scheduler activation flag (sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation under PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq) or slice list (plmnConfigList under PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq, see 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is modified as an on-line change.

If actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled:

L2-PS shall store the information about DRB to NSA resource group association ([Before CNI-116869]resourceGroupId[CNI-116869]dl/ulResourceGroupId[End CNI-116869] parameter) if available. If neither snssai nor resourceGroupId is present within drbAddReqPs, L2-PS shall assume DRB belongs to NSA resource group default for user's PLMN. In that case, L2-PS shall resolve the DRB to NSA resource group association on an as-needed basis in runtime using nsaDefaultResourceGroupId (see 5G_L2_IF_1665_replaced([10969775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ue5ovu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: In context of Slice Aware Scheduler, NSA resource group is referred to as a "slice", see 5G_UP_ALG_7387_replaced([11188675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvd21PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008828-C]

L2-PS should map bearer to the resource group according to 5G_UP_ALG_19736_replaced([11188754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB008709-A](DL), 5G_UP_ALG_23406_replaced([11206779](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwr-1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL) [End CB008709-A].

[End CB008828-C]

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-12 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq DRB mapping based on the optional GBR QOS parameters (ID: 11144174)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11144190`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq drbAddReqPs from 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) indicates the drb configuration parameters. It has optional structures gbrQosSpecificParameters and nonVoNRGbrQosParameters to indicate GBR specific QoS paremeters. The below table indicates how the parameters shall be configured in case of absence / presence of the optional structures.

|  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---  
**GBR 5QI** | **gbrQosSpecificParameters** | **nonVoNRGbrQosParameters** | **GFBR Value Configured** | **IsGbr** | **Is NonVonrGbr**  
5QI-1 **[CB00****8118-A]/65/66**[End CB008118-A]**_*_** * | Present | Present | Non zero | Yes | No  
5QI-1 **[CB008118-A]/65/66**[End CB008118-A]**** | Present | Absent | Not Configured hence use zero | Yes | No  
5QI-1 **[CB008118-A]/65/66**[End CB008118-A]**** | Absent | Absent | Not Configured hence use zero | Yes | No  
5QI-x | Present | Absent | Non zero | No | No  
5QI-x | Absent | Present | Not Configured hence use mingfbr | Yes | Yes  
5QI-x | Absent | Absent | Not Configured | No | No  
5QI-x | Present | Present | Non zero | Yes | Yes  
  
Note : mingfbr shall be set equal to the value of the parameter **rdMinGfbr defined in 5G_L2_4370_replaced([12721757](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_V2dM8G1ZEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))**

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-13 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Configuration of DRB-specific maximum number of HARQ transmissions (ID: 11144196)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11144203`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq For each entry of the drbAddReqPs list field (please see 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received in PsUser_UserSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall store information about optionally configured DRB-specific maximum number of HARQ transmissions for both DL (maxDlHarqTxDrb) and UL (maxUlHarqTxDrb) and use them as input for procedures described in 5G_UP_ALG_12742_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively.

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-17 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Uplink Configured Grant Type 2 Configuration handling (ID: 11144247)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11144253`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq When 5G L2-PS receives a PsUser_UserSetupReq message with the structure "ulCgConfigType2" and the parameter "ulCgConfig" = 1 (CG Configuration) ,

the DL scheduler allocates and stores in UE DL Database a csRnti.

[Before PR700501]

Then, DL scheduler will send an internal message to UL scheduler ("DlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd") that contains as information the csRnti and rnti value.

At reception of internal msg "DlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd" , UL scheduler store csRnti value in UE UL database

[End PR700501]

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-18 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Dedicated UE config state handling on User Setup (ID: 11144261)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11144266`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq L2-PS shall perform following actions:

  * L2-PS shall store in user context optional ueDedicatedConfigState IE value, as received in PsUser_UserSetupReq message. Supported values for ueDedicatedConfigState are:
  * 'disabled (UE has dedicated configuration disabled),
  * not present (UE has dedicated configuration activated).
  * If ueDedicatedConfigState is set to 'disabled', L2-PS shall start transient phase for the user, see 5G_L2_11428_replaced([11170534](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26K3QfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-19 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Handling NBR parameters (ID: 11144273)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-19.0-3**  (ID: `12463102`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserSetupReq message with structure "drbAddReqPs" and if this structure in turn contains structure [Before CB008118-B] "nbrDrbSpecificParams" [CB008118-B] nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams [End CB008118], then the parameters present in structure [Before CB008118-B] "nbrDrbSpecificParams" [CB008118-B] nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams [End CB008118] are stored in ue context. For details of parameters to be stored refer to 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

NBR Congestion Control Priority parameters shall not be present in the nbrDrbSpecificParams received by L2-PS when NBR Congestion control is in deactivated state. L2-PS shall store default values for priority (as defined in 5G_L2_17206_replaced([11177154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_265QCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UE context . The default priority values shall be used for existing UE's / bearer when NBR Congestion control is dynamically enabled and unless the priority is modifed by a separate procedure.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0 (Spare value) , the priority shall be initialized to the default of 14.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 15 (No Priority), the priority value 15 shall be treated lower than the lowest priotiy level (14) for NBR Congestion Control.

---

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-20 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Handling of GBR Congestion control Parameters (ID: 12449451)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-20.0-1**  (ID: `12462994`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserSetupReq message with structure "drbAddReqPs" and if this structure in turn contains structure nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams, then the parameters present in structure nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams are stored in ue context. For details of parameters to be stored refer to 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

GBR Congestion Control Priority parameters shall not be present in the DRB configuration parameter received by L2-PS when GBR Congestion control is in deactivated state. L2-PS shall store default values for priority (as defined in 5G_L2_397_replaced([11151857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24k72fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UE context . The default priority values shall be used for existing UE's / bearer when NBR Congestion control is dynamically enabled and unless the priority is modifed by a separate procedure.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0 (Spare value) , the priority shall be initialized to the default of 14.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 15 (No Priority), the priority value 15 shall be treated lower than the lowest priotiy level (14) for GBR Congestion Control.

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq L2-PS shall store p0 , p0NominalPusch and **[CB015640-A] p0SrsSbBf**[End CB015640-A]from PsUser_UserSetupReq and targetSinrOffset (from PsCell_CellSetupReq, clpcPusch structure see 5G_L2_IF_49_replaced([10966848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQ3OPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_150_replaced([10969724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UeSoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) within UE context in database.****

**2.1.4.1.1.0-23.0-1**  (ID: `12521419`)

FDD SCell use the infromation in the same way as PCell pSRS for critical band impact in [1162192: DL scheduling in overlapping slot with periodic WB TAS SRS for Critical band(txSwitchImpactToRx)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25e6wfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) combing ueCapability->tasSRSImpact->txSwitchImpactToRx as [10975032: ueCapability structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_P9Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).[End CB006139-CG-UPD009]

##### 2.1.4.1.1.0-24 Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq Critical bearer setup during user setup (ID: 13397747)

**2.1.4.1.1.0-24.0-1**  (ID: `13397751`)

Reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq L2-PS shall check the criticality of the bearers requested for setup as mentioned below

  1. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and SRBs part of PsUser_UserSetupReq-> srbAddReqPs[] have their criticalSrbSchedEnabled = True, those respective SRBs are marked as critical SRBs. L2-PS also shall check the DRB criticality to decide the SRB criticality as mentioned in the next steps.



2\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_UserSetupReq-> drbAddReqPs[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as critical DRBs and SRBs.

3\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_UserSetupReq-> drbAddReqPs[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = False, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

4\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = False and SRBs or DRBs part of PsUser_UserSetupReq have their criticality flags criticalSrbSchedEnabled = True or criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, L2-PS shall print a warning message and consider them as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

Note : SRB criticality is decide in three phases.

Phase1 : When there is no DRB. In this phase SRB criticality is decided by its flag criticalSrbSchedEnabled.

Phase2 : When a DRB is setup, SRB criticality is decided by the DRB such that if one or more DRBs are marked with criticalDrbSchedEnabled = true, then the mapping SRB is also considered critical irrespective of its criticalSrbSchedEnabled status.

Phase3: When the last DRB is removed, SRB is considered non critical

---

#### 2.1.4.1.2 Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp

##### 2.1.4.1.2.0-1 Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp Uplink Configured Grant Type 2 Configuration handling (ID: 11144324)

**2.1.4.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11144332`)

Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp csRnti Allocation

---

**2.1.4.1.2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11144343`)

Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp When 5G L2-PS receives PsUser_UserSetupReq message with the structure "ulCgConfigType2" and the parameter "ulCgConfig" = 1 (CG Configuration) and csRnti allocation is done as in 5G_L2_11369, DL scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserSetupResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti).

UL Scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserSetupResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer).

[Before PR700501]

EO SGNL verifies if status of both internal PsUser_UserSetupResp (from DL and UL scheduler) is EStatus5G_OK, and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer) in the message PsUser_UserSetupResp that is sent to CP-RT.

[PR700501]

EO SGNL verifies if status of both internal PsUser_UserSetupResp (from DL and UL scheduler) is EStatus5G_OK, and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer).

Then, Signalling EO will send an internal message to UL scheduler ("SgnlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd") that contains as information the csRnti and rnti value.

At reception of internal msg "SgnlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd" , UL scheduler store csRnti value in UE UL database

Then message PsUser_UserSetupResp that is send to CP-RT.

[End PR700501]

Note: If one of internal PsUser_UserSetupResp has status CgAllocationStatusNOK, the csRnti remains allocated in UE databases until UE Release

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between different components, likely in a cellular network context. The components involved are "UL Scheduler", "DL Scheduler", "SGNL", and "CP-RT". The diagram uses colored boxes to represent these components and arrows to depict messages exchanged between them. Here's a breakdown of the interactions: 1\. **UL Scheduler** initiates a request to **DL Scheduler** with `internal::UserSetupReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`. 2\. **DL Scheduler** has a sub-component called `csRntiAllocator`. It stores `csRnti` in its "DL UE db". 3\. **DL Scheduler** then sends `internal::UserSetupReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)` to **SGNL**. 4\. **UL Scheduler** stores `ulCgConfig`, `ulCgMcsTable`, and `ulCgProfile` in its "UL UE db". It also calls an API `API dB Cell: getCgTimerAndNrOfHarqProcessPair`. 5\. **DL Scheduler** sends `internal::UserSetupResp (Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti))` back to **UL Scheduler**. 6\. **UL Scheduler** then sends `internal::UserSetupResp (Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTime` to **CP-RT**. 7\. **SGNL** is shown to check responses from both schedulers. If everything is okay, it sends `SgnlToUICsrntiAllocationInd` and updates and sends the `UserSetupResp` to **CP-RT**. 8\. **SGNL** receives `internal::SgnlToUICsrntiAllocationInd(rnti, csRnti)`. 9\. **UL Scheduler** stores the received `csRnti` from SGNL and notes that `csRnti` is allocated in the DL scheduler. 10\. Finally, **SGNL** sends `UserSetupResp (OK, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK, csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer))` to **CP-RT**.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_589.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

[https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/CB008124%20-%205G_L2_Entity_Level%20Module%20-%20Drawings/csRnti_IntraScheduler_management.xlsx?d=w46c7c9d4342a456e8e0598c95c60cdb0&csf=1&web=1&e=4MQlKx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level/2%205G-L2-PS%20Component%20Requirements/CB008124%20-%205G_L2_Entity_Level%20Module%20-%20Drawings/csRnti_IntraScheduler_management.xlsx?d=w46c7c9d4342a456e8e0598c95c60cdb0&csf=1&web=1&e=4MQlKx)

**2.1.4.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11144350`)

Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp Exception handling: csRnti Allocation Failure

---

**2.1.4.1.2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11144362`)

Transmission of PsUser_UserSetupResp Exception: csRnti Allocation Failure

L2PS DL scheduler shall consider all the available rnti pools, if the total number of remaining available RNTIs, in percentage, is less than or equal to rdCgMinRntiAvailability (see 5G_UP_ALG_15495_replaced([11173568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuUnUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), CS-RNTI allocation shall be considered as not successful.

L2PS signalling should send UserSetupResp including EStatus5G_OK and ulCgType2AllocationResult structure ( 5G_L2_IF_4389_replaced([10976545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLwvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

> CgAllocationStatus CgAllocationStatusNOK
> 
> CgAllocationCause lackOfCsRnti

Note: If one of internal PsUser_UserSetupResp has status CgAllocationStatusNOK, the csRnti remains allocated in UE databases until UE Release

### 2.1.4.2 User Modify

#### 2.1.4.2.0-3 User Modify Reception of PsUser_UserModifyReq (ID: 11144390)

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11144396`)

User Modify Modification of cell parameters in UE context

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11144437`)

User Modify When 5G-L2-PS receives a UE context modify message with 5G_L2_IF_445_replaced([10975980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEIcvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) procedure, L2-PS shall execute the modification procedure. Currently, only SCell addition, SCell release ,UE cell parameter modification and Scell change are supported.

User Context modification procedure is used also for updating ueCapability parameters received in the User Context setup phase of the SA initial access. Also, ueIdCu parameter that is used for debugging only is updated with the User Context modification procedure (ueIdCu is not known in the User Context setup phase of the SA initial access).

Case the SCell to be released is supported by the L2-RT instance supporting the PCell: To avoid confliction, scheduler need to handle the SCell release first if the numOfScellToRelease is not zero. 5G-L2-PS need to identify the UE context to check whether the serving Cell is existing or not according to its servingCellIndex. If the SCell existed, suspend the DL and UL data on this serving cell, and remove the serving cell information from UE context. For detail of SCell suspend and remove, refer more to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Case the SCell to be released is supported by the L2-RT instance not supporting the PCell (remote SCell): In that case, the pair (numOfRemoteScellToAdd, numOfRemoteScellToRelease) is set to (0,1). The L2-PS Scheduler shall consider that the UE scheduling on the SCell is already stopped. Therefore, the PCell L2-PS scheduler shall no more send or forward any message over the PsPeerCtrl interface. Also, the PCell L2-PS scheduler shall no more schedule any L1 reception of CSI report reception or HARQ feedback for the remote SCell. The PCell L2-PS scheduler shall apply the new PUCCH configuration (parameter pucchConfig) and CSI report configuration (parameter perCsiReportConfig).

Note:

(0,0) is a valid combination for the pair (numOfRemoteScellToAdd, numOfRemoteScellToRelease): the requested modification is not related to remote SCell addition or deletion.

If the numOfRemoteSCellToAdd>0 and numOfRemoteScellToRelease>0, it is FR1 CA Scell change procedure, refer to 5G_L2_632

[CB008140-BB]

When PCell 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserModifyReq message with the Scell in remoteScellToRelease configured as ext-SCell, then it shall send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq with modifType=deactivateExtScell to SCell 5G-L2-PS to deactivate UE in the SCell (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_1143_replaced([11182271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Beq4I_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB008140-BB]

If the numOfSCellToAdd or numOfRemoteSCellToAdd is not zero or the pair (numOfRemoteScellToAdd, numOfRemoteScellToRelease) is set to (1,0), 5G-L2-PS shall identify the UE context according to ueIdDu. 5G-L2-PS shall check whether the servingCellIndex of the UE is used or not and whether the SCell is exist or not.

  * If it is not, UE context shall be updated and serving cell information of the SCell shall be saved. Initial status of the new SCell shall be deactivated and therefore SCell Activation (5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be performed before 5G-L2-PS can start allocating resources on this SCell.

  * Otherwise, it shall be an error case.




If the numOfCellToModify is not zero, which means it is a parameter modification for the cell. Currently only DRX configuration or measurement gap configuration are supported to be modification for the serving cells of UE. Detail processing of DRX configuration of serving cell refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2265_replaced([11114390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Detail processing of measurement gap configuration in SA mode refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4189_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Also srsConfig, perCsiReportConfig, aperiodicCsiConfiguration, pucchConfig, pdschConfig and puschConfig parameter structures for PCell can be added or modified with the User Context modification procedure. If a parameter value was already received during SA initial access upon reception of the User Context setup, it shall be replaced by the value received in the User Context modification procedure. If an optional parameter structure is not included in the User Context modification, the earlier received parameter values shall be kept. Note, if long PUCCH is configured and the UE capability for pi/2 BPSK of PUCCH Format3 is known, then, as defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3941_replaced([11311647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tra7dvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L3_3999_replaced([11032614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BAQdv__KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)), C-Plane might reconfigure IE pi2Bpsk of pucchConfig of pucchFormatConfigF3 together with numOfPrbs of the PUCCH Resource Set1 resources and IE maxNrOfPRBs of perCsiReportConfig. If the IE simultaneousHarqAckCsi in pucchFormatConfigF2 is ”TRUE”, schedule UE with simultaneousHarqAckCsi = true(reference 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise, ignore the IE.

For E-UTRA-NR dual connected UEs, when PsUser_UserModifyReq is received with‘measGapConfig’ structure exist and IE 'measGapConfigStatus' indicates setup, and the configuration of measGapConfig is valid for the UE, 5G-L2-PS shall store these configurations in the UE context and start taking Measurement Gap's influence into account when scheduling this UE. Measurement Gap shall not influence UE's schedule when it is under Random Access (5G_UP_ALG_2291_replaced([11114624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpmfY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). DRX release configuration may be included in the same message, 5G-L2-PS will keep DRX for this UE until the relevant RRC Reconfiguration Complete (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq) is received from CP-RT(5G_UP_ALG_2251_replaced([11114218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpi1CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2265_replaced([11114390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If Carrier Aggregation feature is activated and UE is configured with one or more Scells, all the SCG serving cells of this UE will use the same MG configurations.

For SA, when PsUser_UserModifyReq is received with‘measGapConfig’ structure exist and IE 'measGapConfigStatus' indicates setup, and the configuration of measGapConfig is valid for the UE, 5G-L2-PS shall store these configurations in the UE context and start taking Measurement Gap's influence into account when scheduling this UE.

For E-UTRA-NR dual connected or SA UEs, if MGs have been setup as (5G_UP_ALG_2291_replaced([11114624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpmfY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), when PsUser_UserModifyReq received with‘measGapConfig’ structure exist and IE 'measGapConfigStatus' indicates release, 5G-L2-PS shall release Measurement Gap of this UE when [Before PR673471] the relevant [End PR673471] RRC Reconfiguration Complete (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq) is received from CP-RT(5G_L2_IF_5152_replaced([10977696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VN5gfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [Before PR673471] The relevant here means measGapConfigMode in PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is set to deactivate [End PR673471]

[5GC001013-B] If Carrier Aggregation feature is activated and UE is configured with one or more Scells, all the SCG serving cells of this UE will release the MG at the same time.

If NSA MG are configured from LTE, NR CP-RT may reconfigures CSI feedback related configuration to avoid gap slot. perCsiReportConfig and/or perCsiRsResConfig will be present in PsUser_UserModifyReq, cellConfigurationForModification field in this case.

Only DRX configuration setup and release are supported. DRX configuration shall only be modified in PCell. If it is for DRX setup(drxConfig is present and drxConfig is 1), this user modify message shall not contain other functionality.

5G-L2-PS sends PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP-RT to ACK/NACK corresponding user modification request.

In SA, if fields pdschConfig.beamGroupSize (5G_L2_IF_428_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and perCsiReportConfig.nrOfReportedRS (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are filled in the message, 5G-L2-PS shall store these values in the user context.

  * If actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall send a PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2225_replaced([11113629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * If actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = FALSE, 5G-L2-PS shall send a PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2223_replaced([11113619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



In SA and NSA, if the field beamGroupChangeAck is filled and == FALSE, L2-PS shall re-sent PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2226_replaced([11113639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Here, 5G-L2-PS shall not send PsUser_UserModifyResp.

If a PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq message is received, and if the field beamGroupChangeInd is filled in this message, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as in 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For NSA, if beam reporting is not configured during user setup message, it is configured in user modify message instead when 1st beam group change is triggered

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-1.1**  (ID: `13336704`)

DL HARQ Tx DL HARQ Tx DL HARQ Tx

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-1.1-1**  (ID: `11144444`)

DL HARQ Tx When 5G-L2-PS receives a PsUser_UserModifyReq message with 5G_L2_IF_445_replaced([10975980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEIcvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) procedure, L2-PS shall execute the modification procedure. Currently, only SCell addition, SCell release, UE cell parameter modification and Scell change are supported.

User Context modification procedure is used also for updating ueCapability parameters received in the User Context setup phase of the SA initial access. Also, ueIdCu parameter that is used for debugging only is updated with the User Context modification procedure (ueIdCu is not known in the User Context setup phase of the SA initial access).

[CB008294-A]

In FR2 SA CA, if 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserModifyReq, then 5G-L2-PS shall proceed with any of:

  * reconfiguration of UE context, based on:
  * common UE context parameters,
  * cell specific parameters for already existing cell(s) (PCell and/or SCell(s)), which configuration(s) is/are listed in cellConfigurationForModification,
  * SCell addition procedure for all SCell(s) which configuration(s) is/are listed in cellConfigurationForAddition (see 5G_L2_12994).



[End CB008294-A]

[CNI-99110-F]

For sCellToReleaseList[], cellConfigurationForAddition[], remoteScellToAddList[], remoteScellToReleaseList[] IEs see requirement 5G_L2_14656.

For cellConfigurationForModification[] IE see requirement 5G_L2_14658.

For measGapConfig IE see requirement 5G_L2_14660.

[End CNI-99110-F]

srsConfig IE:

Also srsConfig parameter structures for PCell can be added or modified with the User Context modification procedure. If a parameter value was already received during SA initial access upon reception of the User Context setup, it shall be replaced by the value received in the User Context modification procedure. If an optional parameter structure is not included in the User Context modification, the earlier received parameter values shall be kept.

drxConfig IE:

Only DRX configuration setup and release are supported. DRX configuration shall only be modified in PCell. If it is for DRX setup(drxConfig is present and drxConfig is 1), this user modify message shall not contain other functionality.

[CB008236-B] In addition to DRX configuration setup and release, DRX configuration can be modified from one configuration to another. The new DRX configuraton shall be carried by PsUser_UserModifyReq during L2 triggered transform precoder(TP) ON/OFF rrcReconfiguration procedure, please refer to 5G_L1L2_FLOW_3956_replaced([11181186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BelYkfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In such cases, 5G-L2-PS will not send PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP-RT to ACK/NACK corresponding user modification request. [End CB008236-B]

In SA, if fields pdschConfig.beamGroupSize (5G_L2_IF_428_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and perCsiReportConfig.nrOfReportedRS (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are filled in the message, 5G-L2-PS shall store these values in the user context.

  * If actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch is set to TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall send a PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2225_replaced([11113629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * If actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch is set to FALSE, 5G-L2-PS shall send a PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2223_replaced([11113619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcHXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



In SA and NSA, if the field beamGroupChangeAck is set to FALSE, L2-PS shall resend PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd message as in 5G_UP_ALG_2226_replaced([11113639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Here, 5G-L2-PS shall not send PsUser_UserModifyResp.

[CB008294-A-UPD001] In FR2 SA CA, if 5G-L2-PS instance receives PsUser_UserModifyReq with filled pdschConfig.beamGroupSize during SCell Addition procedure (see 5G_L2_12994), 5G-L2-PS instance shall proceed as in 5G_L2_13802. [End CB008294-A-UPD001]

If a PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq message is received, and if the field beamGroupChangeInd is filled in this message, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as in 5G_UP_ALG_2227_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For NSA, if beam reporting is not configured during PsUser_UserSetupReq, it is configured in PsUser_UserModifyReq instead when 1st beam group change is triggered.

5G-L2-PS sends PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP-RT to ACK/NACK corresponding user modification request.

---

[End CNI-104893-A]

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-1.1.0-1**  (ID: `13336707`)

DL HARQ Tx [image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating the Downlink (DL) Hybrid Automatic Repeat Request (HARQ) Transmission (Tx) process in a 5G system. The diagram depicts interactions between different network entities: UE (User Equipment), 5G-L1-UL (5G Layer 1 Uplink), 5G-L1-DL (5G Layer 1 Downlink), 5G-L2-PS (5G Layer 2 Packet Switched), and 5G-L2-LO (5G Layer 2 Lower Layer). The diagram is divided into two main sections: the initial transmission and retransmissions. **Initial Transmission:** * **5G-L2-PS** initiates the process by performing **DL MAC Scheduling**. * It sends request messages to **5G-L1-DL** and **5G-L1-UL** on a carrier allocation basis. * **5G-L2-LO** assembles the Transport Block (TB) sequentially for each **5G-L1-DL** system component and transmits it on the carrier allocation basis. * **5G-L2-LO** sends a `DIData_PdcchSendReq (DCI)` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** sends a `DIData_PdschSendReq` to **5G-L2-PS**. * **5G-L2-PS** sends a `LoCtrl_PduMuxReq` to **5G-L2-LO**. * **5G-L2-LO** sends a `DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq (DL HARQ Tx)` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** sends `PDCCH` and `PDSCH (TB)` to the **UE**. * The **UE** receives the data and sends back `UIData_PucchReceiveReq` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** then sends `UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs` and `UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD` to **5G-L2-PS**. * The DL HARQ feedback of all configured Component Carriers (CCs) in the UE (Joint-UCI) is received via the **5G-L1** of the UE's PSCell. **Retransmission (Loop):** The diagram indicates an optional loop that continues "until HARQ ACK is received OR numOfTx reaches maxDIHarqTx". * **DL HARQ ReTx in case of HARQ N** : This section details the retransmission process. * **5G-L2-PS** performs **DL MAC Scheduling** again. * It sends `DIData_PdcchSendReq (DCI)` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** sends `DIData_PdschSendReq` to **5G-L2-PS**. * **5G-L2-PS** sends `LoCtrl_PduMuxReq` to **5G-L2-LO**. * **5G-L2-LO** sends `DIData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq (DL HARQ ReTx)` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** sends `PDCCH` and `PDSCH (TB ReTx)` to the **UE**. * The **UE** receives the retransmitted data and sends back `UIData_PucchReceiveReq` to **5G-L1-DL**. * **5G-L1-DL** then sends `UIData_PucchReceiveRespPs` and `UIData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD` to **5G-L2-PS**. A note indicates that HARQ retransmission is done via the same **5G-L1** where the original transmission was done.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m1dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_Flows_file_2385.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Link to the "5G_L1L2_FLOW_260_DL HARQ Tx.signalling" file:

[https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L1%20and%20L2%20Entity%20Level%20Flows/8%20User%20Plane%20Data%20Transfer/8.1%20DL%20Data%20Transfer%20(MAC%20level)/5G_L1L2_FLOW_260_DL%20HARQ%20Tx.signalling?csf=1&web=1&e=WAmCeg](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20L1%20and%20L2%20Entity%20Level%20Flows/8%20User%20Plane%20Data%20Transfer/8.1%20DL%20Data%20Transfer%20\(MAC%20level\)/5G_L1L2_FLOW_260_DL%20HARQ%20Tx.signalling?csf=1&web=1&e=WAmCeg)

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11144477`)

DL HARQ Tx sCellToReleaseList[], cellConfigurationForAddition[], remoteScellToAddList[], remoteScellToReleaseList[] IEs

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11144482`)

DL HARQ Tx Case the SCell to be released is supported by the L2-RT instance supporting the PCell: To avoid confliction, scheduler need to handle the SCell release first if the size of scellToReleaseList is not zero. 5G-L2-PS need to identify the UE context to check whether the serving Cell is existing or not according to its servingCellIndex. If the SCell existed, suspend the DL and UL data on this serving cell, and remove the serving cell information from UE context. For detail of SCell suspend and remove, refer more to 5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Case the SCell to be released is supported by the L2-RT instance not supporting the PCell (remote SCell): In that case, the pair (size of remoteSCellToAddList, size of remoteScellToRelease) is set to (0,1). The L2-PS Scheduler shall consider that the UE scheduling on the SCell is already stopped. Therefore, the PCell L2-PS scheduler shall no more send or forward any message over the PsPeerCtrl interface. Also, the PCell L2-PS scheduler shall no more schedule any L1 reception of CSI report reception or HARQ feedback for the remote SCell. The PCell L2-PS scheduler shall apply the new PUCCH configuration (parameter pucchConfig) and CSI report configuration (parameter perCsiReportConfig).

Note:

(0,0) is a valid combination for the pair (size of remoteSCellToAddList, size of remoteScellToRelease): the requested modification is not related to remote SCell addition or deletion.

If the size of remoteSCellToAddList is greater than 0 and size of remoteScellToRelease is greater than 0, it is FR1 CA Scell change procedure, refer to 5G_L2_632.

When PCell 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserModifyReq message with the Scell in remoteScellToRelease configured as ext-SCell, then it shall send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq with modifType=deactivateExtScell to SCell 5G-L2-PS to deactivate UE in the SCell (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_1143_replaced([11182271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Beq4I_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If the cellConfigurationForAddition is not empty or size of remoteSCellToAddList is not zero or the pair (size of remoteSCellToAddList, size of remoteScellToRelease) is set to (1,0), 5G-L2-PS shall identify the UE context according to ueIdDu. 5G-L2-PS shall check whether the servingCellIndex of the UE is used or not and whether the SCell is exist or not.

  * If it is not, UE context shall be updated and serving cell information of the SCell shall be saved. Initial status of the new SCell shall be deactivated and therefore SCell Activation (5G_UP_ALG_2778_replaced([11120862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqU4JfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be performed before 5G-L2-PS can start allocating resources on this SCell.

  * Otherwise, it shall be an error case.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11144490`)

DL HARQ Tx cellConfigurationForModification[] IE

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12786907`)

DL HARQ Tx Elements of the _cellConfigurationForModification are related to PCell and/or SCell(s) and are used to modify these cell(s). Currently only DRX configuration or measurement gap configuration are supported to be modification for the serving cells of UE. Detail processing of DRX configuration of serving cell refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2265_replaced([11114390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Detail processing of measurement gap configuration in SA mode refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4189_replaced([11174355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

Also ~~srsConfig,~~ _perCsiReportConfig,_ aperiodicCsiConfiguration, _pucchConfig,_ pdschConfig and _puschConfig parameter structures for PCell can be added or modified with the User Context modification procedure. If a parameter value was already received during SA initial access upon reception of the User Context setup, it shall be replaced by the value received in the User Context modification procedure. If an optional parameter structure is not included in the User Context modification, the earlier received parameter values shall be kept. Note, if long PUCCH is configured and the UE capability for pi/2 BPSK of PUCCH Format3 is known, then, as defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_3941_replaced([11311647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tra7dvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L3_3999_replaced([11032614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BAQdv__KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)), C-Plane might reconfigure IE pi2Bpsk of pucchConfig of _pucchFormatConfigF3 together with numOfPrbs of the PUCCH Resource Set1 resources and IE maxNrOfPRBs of _perCsiReportConfig. If the IE_ simultaneousHarqAckCsi in _pucchFormatConfigF2 is_ TRUE, schedule UE with _simultaneousHarqAckCsi =_ TRUE (reference 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise ignore the IE.**_*_** *****

_cellConfigurationForModification IE can be used to reconfigure the MCS table in the Scell between qam64LowSE and qam64/qam256[CB008949-C]/qam1024[End CB008949-C]. As for the MCS table reconfiguation on Pcell, at reception of PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq, the Scell shall take the new configured MCS table into use._

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11144509`)

DL HARQ Tx remoteScellToModifyList[]

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13329576`)

DL HARQ Tx When step-wise scell addition to CA UE, the UE's retaineded SCell may be reconfigured. If UE's retained SCell is reconfigured and the parameter in structure RemoteSCellModifyParam is being changed, the SCell should be included in _remoteScellToModifyList[], and the new value of these parameters should be informed to PCell in this structure for the SCell._

[CB010741-C]  
In case of SCell upgrade of DL_Only retained SCell to DL_UL, the SCell should be included in remoteScellToModifyList[] with caConfigDU set to DL_UL (Ref: 10976333) with all the remaining configuration parameters. This configuration parameters are used by PCell to upgrade the SCell as DL_UL capable.  
[End CB010741-C]

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11144522`)

DL HARQ Tx step-wise SCell addition to a CA UE

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11144527`)

DL HARQ Tx When step-wise scell addition to CA UE, the UE in PsUser_UserModifyReq should has at least one SCell configured already before the message, and PsUser_UserModifyReq should have one new SCell in remoteSCelltoAddList[], while no scell in remoteScellToRelease[].

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `13336155`)

DL HARQ Tx step-wise SCell Upgrade of DL_Only to DL_UL to a CA UE

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13336156`)

DL HARQ Tx When SCell upgrade triggered for a CA UE, the UE in PsUser_UserModifyReq should have this SCell configured with DL_Only before the message , and PsUser_UserModifyReq should not have any new SCell in remoteSCelltoAddList[], and no scell in remoteScellToRelease[].

PsUser_UserModifyReq towards PCell will be with ueModifyCause=pcellModForScellUpgrade  
PsUser_UserModifyReq towards SCell with ueModifyCause=RetainedScellModWhileStepWiseScellAddOrUpgrade.

PsUser_UserModifyReq will include related UL Configurations needed to be updated (ex: IE’s in cellConfigModifyParam, UE's UL Specific parameters) for to-be-upgrade SCell. CellConfigModifyParam ([10976438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VGkufu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) will indicate SCell upgrade with caConfigDU set to DL_UL

Note: Ref: [13325677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DskKsNK3EfCnq6aYkXj8Pw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) For flow diag

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `12480814`)

DL HARQ Tx **retained SCell reconfiguration when step-wise SCell addition or SCell Upgrade to a CA UE**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `13336964`)

DL HARQ Tx When step-wise scell addition to CA UE [CB010741-C] OR SCell Upgrade[End CB010741-C], if SCell receives PsUser_UserModifyReq with _ueModifyCause = [Before CB010741-C]RetainScellModWhileStepWiseScellAdd [CB010741-C]RetainScellModWhileStepWiseScellAddOrUpgrade [End CB010741-C]as 5G_L2_IF_453_replaced([10976074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEvgvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the SCell should not schedule any PDSCH or PUSCH before corresponding PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq._

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11144536`)

DL HARQ Tx **possible periodic SRS reconfiguration from TDD SCell**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11144543`)

DL HARQ Tx For FDD PCell, when TDD SCell's pSRS is reconfigured on period or on SRS symbol due to [11153999: Modification of SRS configuration and activation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspza_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA), then on the legacy configured and new configured TDD PSRS slot:

If the UE does not enter UL transient phase as [11194889: Reception of PsUser_UserModifyReq without UE dedicated configuration update indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9),

the PUSCH scheduled shall use shortest usable slot duration with consideration that UL TX Switch before reconfiguration or after reconfiguration is on, then UL TX Switch is on;

else

the PUSCH shall not be scheduled.

endif

And number of PUCCH symbols may be reconfigured when TDD SCell pSRS symbol position change according to [11187168: PUCCH configuration for CA UE with FDD P(S)Cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-XPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA), and the transient phase behavior should as [11177778: PUCCH resource selection for FDD + TDD FR1 UL Tx switching UE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kux6U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `11144548`)

DL HARQ Tx **parameter reconfiguration when step-wise SCell addition OR SCell Upgrade (DL to DL_UL) to a CA UE**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `13336196`)

DL HARQ Tx [When step-wise scell addition [CB010741-C] OR SCell Upgrade [End CB010741-C] to CA UE, the UE in PsUser_UserModifyReq may be newly configured [CB010741-C] OR its existing SCell being Upgraded to DL_UL [End CB010741-C]:

  1. _ulTxSwitch reconfigured_ in _cellConfigurationForModification[] [CB010741-C] or present in_ remoteScellToModifyList[] during SCell upgrade[End CB010741-C]_for PCell and DL-UL SCell:_ ****



When _ulTxSwitch is present, the UE's UL TX Switch is reconfigured. The dedicate pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList on FDD UL serving cell may be impacted considering critical band impact on PUSCH(_ tasSRSImpact _._ txSwitchWithAnotherBand) from TDD PCell and p-SRS configuration on TDD serving SCell, refer to 5G_UP_11397_replaced([11356891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uca_JfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_11461. **If _ulTxSwitch is reconfigured from disable to enable, when the FDD serving cell's pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList is impacted, it should be sent by PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP; if ulTxSwitch is reconfigured from enable to disable, even if some element of pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList shall not be used, the pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList is not updated, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_6571_replaced([11115928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpzTt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). And if the impacted serving cell is PCell, UE should enter transient phase as 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **See also Note2._******* *

**Note 1: On TDD CC, if ultxSwitch is enabled, adaptive SRS can't be triggered as 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

  1. _ulCa3Tx reconfigured in_ cellConfigurationForModification[] [CB010741-C] or present in  _remoteScellToModifyList[] during SCell upgrade[End CB010741-C]_ for PCell and DL-UL SCell:****



When _ulCa3Tx is present, the UE's ulCa3Tx is reconfigured. The reconfigured parameter should be taken into use after the corresponding RrcReconfCompletedReq to L2-PS. For TDD PCell, with_ ulCa3Tx reconfigured to enable, should check the latest parameter as 5G_L2_656 and 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to enable or disable adaptive SRS; if _ulCa3Tx reconfigured from enable to disable while there is still UL CA, adaptive SRS is not supported on TDD PCell according to 5G_L3_2955_replaced([11028803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_3cMv_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))._**

  1. retained SCell reconfiguration to PCell:



When retained SCell is reconfigured, except the SCell's perCsiReportConfig in PCell's _cellConfigurationForModification its reconfiguration which is needed by PCell is passed by_ remoteScellToModifyList[] in PCell's PsUser_UserModifyReq. Upon receiving _remoteScellToModifyList[] , L2-PS should use parmeter in_ perCsiReportConfig and _remoteScellToModifyList to check if the bit number of the Scell's PCSI/BM report is impacted as 5G_UP_ALG_12845_replaced([11159141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktHtdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the bit number of the Scell's PCSI/BM report is impacted, PCell should exclude UE's scheduling as 5G_UP_ALG_4196_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4826_replaced([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). L2PS should take the reconfigured SCell's parameter into usage after the corresponding RrcReconfCompletedReq to L2-PS, and the impacted PCSI/BM report should be ignored during the before PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq._****

When the retained TDD DL-UL SCell's periodic SRS is reconfigured while step-wise SCell addition [CB010741-C] or TDD DL SCell's periodic SRS is configured during SCell upgrade [CB010741-C] , i.e. _remoteScellToModifyList[] for the SCell includes_ numOfPerSrsRes, if the SRS resource is reconfigured from no SRS to with SRS, or from with SRS to no SRS, the pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList is not impacted by pSRS due to [1115859: Default TDRA list](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpyspPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA). But if FDD PCell's schedule is impacted by the overall reconfiguration, do the scheduling according to [11144536: possible periodic SRS reconfiguration from TDD SCell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_236Ne_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). See also Note2.**

The TDD DL-UL SCell should not receive pSRS when it is being reconfigured before PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq. 

When UL TX Switch is reconfigured, the FDD PCell scheduling is as [11144536: possible periodic SRS reconfiguration from TDD SCell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_236Ne_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). Several examples are as bellow:

  1. PCell reconfiguration to SCell:



When retained SCell is reconfigured for a CA UE by PsUser_UserModifyReq, the PCell's parameter is in _cellConfigurationForModification[0] of the PsUser_UserModifyReq for the Scell, and remotePcellToModify if present:_

The Scell should use _perCsiReportConfig in_ cellConfigurationForModification[0] for the SCell to handle its PCSI/BM report. The new parameter should be taken into use after the corresponding RrcReconfCompletedReq to L2-PS, and the impacted PCSI/BM report with bit number change should be ignored before PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq.**

If the TDD PCell's periodic SRS is reconfigured from no pSRS to with pSRS, or from with pSRS to no pSRS, the FDD DL-UL SCell's pdschTimeDomainAllocationList is not impacted by pSRS due to only TAS pSRS symbol 12 is supported according to 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_13750_replaced([11329463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtDTLfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList should be updated according to [11115992: Dedicate entry for FR1 UL Tx Switching in FDD Cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

If PCell's critical band impact releated to TAS pSRS is reconfigured, informing SCell by PsUser_UserModifyReq->ueCapability->tasSRSImpact:

∙ if PsUser_UserModifyReq->ueCapability->tasSRSImpact->txSwitchImpactToRx is changed from FALSE to TRUE, the FDD SCell may need to recalculate its pdschTimeDomainAllocationList according to 5G_L2_15411; if it is changed from TRUE to FALSE, the pdschTimeDomainAllocationList is not updated;

∙ if PsUser_UserModifyReq->ueCapability->tasSRSImpact->txSwitchWithAnotherBand is changed from FALSE to TRUE, the FDD DL-UL SCell may need recalculate its pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList according to 5G_L2_11462 by combining the UlTxSwitch configuration; if it is changed from TRUE to FALSE, the pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList is not updated;

**See also Note2.**

  1. PCell reconfiguration handling



For PCell's reconfiguration for PCell itself, no new parameters introduced by step-wise Scell addition [CB010741-C] or SCell Upgrade scenario [CB010741-C] except 1, 2, 3, so any other parameter reconfiguration except 1, 2, 3, should be handled as 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_8181_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4826_replaced([11195069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv5UqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4196_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note 2: bellow is an illustration on how the symbol should be shortened on FDD serving cell when ulTxSwitch or tasSRSImpact or pSRS is reconfigured in 1,3,4 when the FDD PCell symbol 13 is overlapped with TDD SCell pSRS:**

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `11144579`)

DL HARQ Tx measGapConfig IE

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11144591`)

DL HARQ Tx For E-UTRA-NR dual connected UEs, when PsUser_UserModifyReq is received with measGapConfig structure exist and IE measGapConfigStatus indicates setup, and the configuration of measGapConfig is valid for the UE, 5G-L2-PS shall store these configurations in the UE context and start taking Measurement Gap's influence into account when scheduling this UE. Measurement Gap shall not influence UE's schedule when it is under Random Access (5G_UP_ALG_2291_replaced([11114624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpmfY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For SA, when PsUser_UserModifyReq is received with measGapConfig structure exist and IE measGapConfigStatus indicates setup, and the configuration of measGapConfig is valid for the UE, 5G-L2-PS shall store these configurations in the UE context and start taking Measurement Gap's influence into account when scheduling this UE.

For E-UTRA-NR dual connected or SA UEs, if MGs have been setup as (5G_UP_ALG_2291_replaced([11114624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpmfY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), when PsUser_UserModifyReq received with measGapConfig structure exist and IE measGapConfigStatus indicates release, 5G-L2-PS shall release Measurement Gap of this UE when RRC Reconfiguration Complete (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq) is received from CP-RT(5G_L2_IF_5152_replaced([10977696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VN5gfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CNI-104893-A]

DRX release configuration may be included in the same message with measGap setup configuration, 5G-L2-PS will keep DRX for this UE until the relevant RRC Reconfiguration Complete (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq) is received from CP-RT(5G_UP_ALG_2251_replaced([11114218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpi1CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_2265_replaced([11114390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpkDLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CNI-104893-A]

If NSA MG are configured from LTE, NR CP-RT may reconfigures CSI feedback related configuration to avoid gap slot. perCsiReportConfig and/or perCsiRsResConfig will be present in PsUser_UserModifyReq, cellConfigurationForModification field in this case.

If any of perSrConfig parameter changed [CB009189-A], except the case when the only changed parameter is payloadSizeSr [End CB009189-A] and the PUCCH mode is long PUCCH, L2-PS shall start Scheduling Request reconfiguration transient phase for a UE.

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-12**  (ID: `11144617`)

DL HARQ Tx Adding dedicated BWPs

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-12.0-3**  (ID: `11144636`)

DL HARQ Tx This requirement is valid if PsUser_UserModifyReq.ueDedicatedConfigState is not present.  
if PsUser_UserModifyReq.ueDedicatedConfigState is present, the relevant requirement is 5G_L2_11424.

L2PS shall start transient phase for a UE, if PsUser_UserModifyReq modifies number of dedicated BWPs in PCell from one to more.

During transient phase only DCI 0_0 and 1_0 on CSS (PDCCH-Type3) are in use.  
See transient phase descriptions in: 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4196_replaced([11174380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kubVCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4045_replaced([11168583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3937_replaced([11168480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB013742-A]**

During transient phase, L2-PS shall also follow the DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure specified by 5G_L2_22365.

**[End CB013742-A]**

L2PS shall finish transient phase if PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is received **[CB013742-A] or completion of DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013742-A].****

**[CB013742-A]**

During transient phase, L2-PS shall also follow the DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure specified by 5G_L2_22365.

**[End CB013742-A]**

L2PS shall finish transient phase if PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is received **[CB013742-A] or completion of DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013742-A].****

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-16**  (ID: `11144691`)

DL HARQ Tx Dedicated UE config state handling on User Modify

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-16.0-3**  (ID: `11144712`)

DL HARQ Tx L2-PS shall perform following actions:

  * L2-PS shall store in user context optional ueDedicatedConfigState IE value, as received in PsUser_UserModifyReq message. Supported values for ueDedicatedConfigState are:



o 'disabled' (UE has dedicated configuration disabled)

o 'inProgress' dedicated configuration disabled or dedicated configuration activated,

o not present (UE has dedicated configuration activated).

  * If ueDedicatedConfigState is set to 'disabled' or 'inProgress', and current setting in the user context is not 'activated', **L2-PS shall continue transient phase for the user, see 5G_L2_11428.**
  * If ueDedicatedConfigState is set to 'inProgress' and current setting in the user context is 'activated', L2-PS shall start transient phase for the user, see 5G_L2_17046.
  * If ueDedicatedConfigState is set to 'inProgress', L2-PS shall start DL SRB1 buffer monitoring procedure for detection of activation of UE dedicated configuration (via RRC Reconfiguration), see 5G_L2_11483, 5G_UP_ALG_18234_replaced([11153699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksn-OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * **[CB013742-A] If ueDedicatedConfigState is not present and**[Before CB013742-SR-C] rrmRrcReconfigurationNeeded **[CB013742-SR-C] isMacLayerMonitorNeeded**[End CB013742-SR-C] is evaluated as ‘TRUE’ according to 5G _L2_22352 (RRC Reconfiguration is needed after user modify request), L2-PS shall start DL SRB1 buffer monitoring procedure specified in 5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). UE dedicated configuration activation status is not affected in this situation. **[End CB013742-A]****_*_** *

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-17**  (ID: `11144717`)

DL HARQ Tx maxDataRateDl handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11144724`)

DL HARQ Tx When L2-PS receives maxDataRateDl it shall save it as it's been received on the Component Carrier level. In case of CA each CC value shall be used for any further calculation.

For the legacy functionality of FR2 CA LP-PS shall use CC level of maxDataRateDl provided by CP-RT and calculate the sum of all CC values to simulate the previous single UE value approach.

DL HARQ Tx When L2-PS receives maxNumOfDlLayers it shall save it as it's been received on the Component Carrier level. In case of CA each CC value shall be used for any further calculation.

For the legacy functionality of FR2 CA only a single CC value shall be used from cellConfiguration[0].pdschConfig, CP-RT shall provide the same value for all CC in such configuration.

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-19**  (ID: `11144749`)

DL HARQ Tx transformPrecoderSwitch handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-19.0-4**  (ID: `11144777`)

DL HARQ Tx Transform precoder reconfiguration Start:

The request to enable or disable the transform precoder is indicated by CP-RT through message PsUser_UserModifyReq by setting IE l2psRequiredIndTrigger is transformPrecoderSwith.

The same message can request to reconfigure the UL MCS Table (puschConfig.mcsTable) and puschConfig.betaOffsetConfig.

Transform precoder reconfiguration CANCELLATION:

L2-PS can receive the request to cancel a previous transform precoder reconfiguration request (e.g. due to unsuccessful completion of the RRC reconfiguration, see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_133_replaced([11180124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5BfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L3_FLOW_22741). The cancellation command is indicated via message PsUser_UserModifyReq by setting [Before CB007880-A]L2psRequiredIndCancellation [CB007880-A] cancellationType [End CB007880-A]is transformPrecoderSwith

The cancellation request shall also contain cellConfigurationForModification IE for the relevant cell and puschConfig IE with the parameter values of 'old' DMRS configuration (i.e. prior the configuration was potentially modified by a previous PsUser_UserModifyReq, which started the current transition phase) for the modification revert.

Rationale: 5G-L2-PS instance modifies the UL DMRS configuration for a given UE and cell by updating a UE context after the instance receives a PsUser_UserModifyReq message which contains puschConfig, without waiting for a successful completion of a UE/RRC reconfiguration procedure, which triggered sending of the PsUser_UserModifyReq message, which in turn started a transition phase. The instance does not keep (store in a memory) the 'old' DMRS configuration of the UE context during the transition phase, and the new DMRS configuration becomes effective when 5G-L2-PS leaves the transition phase.

The cancellation request shall contain the ‘old’ UL MCS Table (puschConfig.mcsTable) and puschConfig.betaOffsetConfig which L2-PS should revert to, if the initial TP reconfiguration request (PsUser_UserModifyReq.transformPrecoderSwitchAck = true) required also a reconfiguration of these parameter (see 5G_L3_FLOW_81708)

After PsUser_UserModifyReq with [Before CB007880-A] l2psRequiredIndCancellation [CB007880-A]cancellationType [End CB007880-A] is transformPrecoderSwith, no PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is expected (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_3683_replaced([11180113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5BPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Refer to requirements 5G_L2_652 and 5G_L2_654 for the description of the actions taken by L2-PS in the different cases.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-20**  (ID: `11144786`)

DL HARQ Tx Slot Aggrgation Switch Handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-20.0-1**  (ID: `11144792`)

DL HARQ Tx Slot Aggrgation reconfiguration Start:

When a UE has a VoNR bearer with the "actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl" parameter set to "True",

The request to enable or disable the Slot Aggrgation is indicated by CP-RT through message PsUser_UserModifyReq by setting IE l2psRequiredIndTrigger is slotAggregationSwitch.

Slot Aggrgation reconfiguration CANCELLATION:

L2-PS can receive the request to cancel a previous Slot Aggrgation reconfiguration request (e.g. due to unsuccessful completion of the RRC reconfiguration, see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_133_replaced([11180124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5BfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L3_FLOW_22741). The cancellation command is indicated via message PsUser_UserModifyReq by setting cancellationType is slotAggregationSwitch

The cancellation request shall also contain cellConfigurationForModification IE for the relevant cell and puschConfig IE with the parameter values of 'old' DMRS configuration (i.e. prior the configuration was potentially modified by a previous PsUser_UserModifyReq, which started the current transition phase) for the modification revert.

After PsUser_UserModifyReq with cancellationType is slotAggregationSwitch, no PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is expected (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_3683_replaced([11180113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5BPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Refer to requirements 5G_L2_12671,5G_L2_23912 and 5G_L2_23914 for the description of the actions taken by L2-PS in the different cases.

Note: Transform Precoder Switching Decision still holds good for decision of slot aggregation on to off vice versa when a UE configured forced TP State.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-21**  (ID: `11144799`)

DL HARQ Tx Forced transformPrecoder handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-21.0-2**  (ID: `12802895`)

DL HARQ Tx When a UE has a VoNR bearer with the "actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl" parameter set to "True" within the drbAddReqPs message (Disabled to Enabled)

If CP-RT send the Forced Transform Precoding request (PsUser_UserModifyReq->2psRequiredIndTrigger is forcedTransformPrecoder, L2-PS shall:

  * Start timer rdTransformPrecodeRrcReconfigTimer (5G_L2_1461);

  * Enter the reconfiguration transient phase;




The request is to enable the transform precoder is indicated by the CP-RT through the PsUser_UserModifyReq message with setting "forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch" as True ,L2-PS shall responds PsUser_UserModifyRes with [Before CNI-134949-A] puschTdraConfigSet [CNI-134949-A] puschTimeDomainAllocationList and puschTimeDomainAllocationListR16 [End CNI-134949-A] as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_7087_replaced([11171627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF92vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and update number of SRS Port as specified 5G_UP_ALG_6925_replaced([11157717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: In order to avoid possible conflicts between DCI 0_0 size and DCI 0_1 size due to the Reconfiguration, L2-PS shall manage the size of the PUSCH TDRA Table as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_7087_replaced([11171627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF92vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see also 5G_UP_ALG_7115_replaced([11171588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuFW0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). When the transient phase is left after a cancellation of the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch = CANCELLATION), L2-PS shall apply the PUSCH TDRA Table which was in use before the re-configuration.

L2-PS shall apply requirements 5G_L2_652 and 5G_L2_654 for the description of the actions taken by L2-PS in the different cases applied only incase If UE is eligible for SlotAggeration as specified 5G_L2_12671 post completion of RRC Reconfig Complete Indication.

Exceptional handling ,Existing parameters should be maintained at its current value if the TP is switched from disabled to enabled by the CP-RT due to the addition of a 5QI-1 DRB and the "actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl" parameter is set to TRUE. In this scenario, the "cancellationType" parameter should be set to "forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch"(Refer to 5G_L2_7543) and communicated to the 5G-L2PS via the PsUser_UserModifyReq message.

When a UE has a VoNR bearer with the "actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl" parameter set to "True" within the drbAddReqPs message (Enabled to Disabled )

The request is to disable the transform precoder is indicated by the CP-RT through the PsUser_UserSetupReq or PsUser_UserModifyReq message by setting the "forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch" as False, L2-PS shall disable Forced TP ON state.

If CP-RT indicates that the RRC Reconfiguration has been completed succesfully (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq->transformPrecoderSwitchInd = success) L2-PS shall:

  * Set the UE to Transform Precoder Enabled state;

  * stop timer rdTransformPrecodeRrcReconfigTimer and exit the transient phase.

  * L2-PS shall apply and resume requirements 5G_L2_652 and 5G_L2_654 for the description of the actions taken by L2-PS in the different cases post completion of RRC Reconfig Complete Indication.




else if CP-RT request to cancel the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->l2psRequiredIndCancellation is forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch, L2-PS shall:

  * Set UE back to Transform Precoder Disabled state;

  * stop timer rdTransformPrecodeRrcReconfigTimer and exit the transient phase;

  * stop the DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure in case of it is started (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




Exceptional handling ,Existing parameters should be maintained at its current value if the TP is switched from enabled to disabled or vice versa by the CP-RT due to the release of a 5QI-1 DRB and the "actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl" parameter is set to FALSE. When the transient phase is left after a cancellation of the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->forcedTransformPrecoderSwitch = CANCELLATION), L2-PS shall apply the PUSCH TDRA Table which was in use before the re-configuration..

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-26**  (ID: `11144880`)

-set Ue status to reestablishment transient phase both UL and DL.

-UL and DL exit reestablishment transient phase.

the DL scheduler allocates and stores in UE DL Database a csRnti.

[Before PR700501]

At reception of internal msg "DlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd" , UL scheduler store csRnti value in UE UL database

[End PR700501]

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-32**  (ID: `11144973`)

DL HARQ Tx Abort and rollback ongoing MCS-table reconfiguration

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-32.0-2**  (ID: `11144987`)

DL HARQ Tx L2-PS shall support the abortion/rollback of an on-going user modify procedure if this procedure was meant for:  
\- MCS table reconfiguration from QAM64 to LowSE for switching to High Reliability Link Adaptation

  * MCS table reconfiguration from LowSE to QAM64 for switching to Basic Reliability Link Adaptation



See 5G_L3_FLOW_78954 for the applicable message sequence chart.

Along with the aforementioned MCS table reconfiguration the betaOffset(~Config) values of structure puschConfig may be reconfigured in Pcell and Scell.

Note, a user modify procedure is considered on-going if the PsUser_RrcReconfigCompleteReq message has not been received yet **[CB013742-A] and DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not completed, **[End CB013742-A] such that the user is still in the transient phase.****

The rollback procedure is triggered by a PsUser_UserModifyReq in which the parameter MCS-table of PdschConfig or PuschConfig of PsUser_UserModifyReq is set to ‘cancelMcsTableReconfiguration’.

At reception L2-PS shall immediately stop the on-going transient phase handling **[CB013742-A] including the DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure in case of it is started (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013742-A], like e.g. stop forced usage of DCIs 0_0 and 1_0 incl. HARQ buffer flushing (5G_UP_ALG_8181_replaced([11153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_5074_replaced([11202363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwcuSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and apply the initial MCS-table again. As the same message contains the old betaOffset values L2-PS shall apply them immediately.****

There won’t be any PsUser_RrcReconfigCompleteReq, i.e. rollback procedure ends with PsUser_UserModifyResp message sent back to L3.

For the same MCS-table reconfiguration cases mentioned above, the rollback shall be supported also on the Scell. The rollback on the Scell is triggered separately and in the same way as in the Pcell. At reception of the cancellation request related to the Scell, L2-PS shall take the same actions as for the Pcell to restore old MCS table and betaOffset.

As a general note for implementation, it is expected that this message only rolls back changes of parameters which support roll-back by specific flags (like MCS-table) and which were done by the previous user modify request message, i.e. there won't be a reconfiguration of parameters that haven’t been modified by the previous message.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-33**  (ID: `11144993`)

DL HARQ Tx Response for L2-PS triggered User Reconfiguration Required

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-33.0-1**  (ID: `11145000`)

DL HARQ Tx CP-RT send PsUser_UserModifyReq with IE l2psRequiredIndTrigger as reponse of L2-PS triggered User Reconfiguration Required procedure.

If IE l2psRequiredIndTrigger is represent, there is ongoing procedure trigged by L2-PS (see 5G_L2_IF_536_replaced([10977582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VNSbfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). L2-PS handle it based on different trigger.

If L2-PS received PsUser_UserModifyReq with IE l2psRequiredIndCancellation, it represents that "L2-PS has received PsUser_UserModifyReq with IE l2psRequiredIndTrigger" already, L2-PS shall rollback to previous configuration and cancel Reconfiguration based on value of l2psRequiredIndCancellation.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-34**  (ID: `11145006`)

DL HARQ Tx Anticipated UL grant

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-34.0-2**  (ID: `11145021`)

DL HARQ Tx [Before CNI-127390-D]

When 5G-L2-PS received a valid PsUser_UserModifyReq message with ueRRCReconfigurationNotNeeded set to false it shall:

· raise dedicated warning that 5G-CP-RT send unexpected value, and

· response with PsUser_UserModifyResp (see 5G_L2_IF_5164_replaced([10976511](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VGkw_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with status set to Estatus5G_notOk

Note: RRC processing delay for AUG SRB is applicable on PCell only. For SCell is not applicable due to no SRB messages on SCell.

[End CNI-127390-D]
