**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-35**  (ID: `11145029`)

DL HARQ Tx **MAC Layer Monitoring for RRC Reconfiguration setting**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-35.0-3**  (ID: `12793199`)

DL HARQ Tx L2-PS shall evaluate isMacLayerMonitorNeeded after user modify procedure and save it for later usage.

  * TRUE: MAC Layer Monitoring for RRC Reconfiguration is needed

  * FALSE: MAC Layer Monitoring for RRC Reconfiguration is not needed




If all below conditions are satisfied, isMacLayerMonitorNeeded shall be evaluated as TRUE; else, isMacLayerMonitorNeeded shall be evaluated as FALSE:

\- rrmEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom is set to 'TRUE' (5G_L2_22348_replaced([11142460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23unR_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_22350_replaced([11143101](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23yRqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

\- Current UE is a SA UE (PsUser_UserSetupReq::callType is set to “CT_SAInitialAccess”). Informatively, L2-PS SW further checks whether SRB1 bear is configured to this UE to determine it is a SA UE.

\- Current UE is not a SCell UE (PsUser_UserSetupReq::ueAddCause is not set to “SCellAddition”)

\- cookie is not present in PsUser_UserModifyReq

\- cancellationType is not present in PsUser_UserModifyReq

\- the parameter MCS-table of PdschConfig or PuschConfig is not set to ‘cancelMcsTableReconfiguration’

\- [CB011022-CB] the parameter dmrsType of PdschConfig is not set to ‘cancelDmrsTypeReconfiguration’ [End CB011022-CB]

\- ueDedicatedConfigState is not present in PsUser_UserModifyReq

\- perSrConfigChangeRollback is not present in PsUser_UserModifyReq

\- ueSssNotAdded is false or not present in PsUser_UserModifyReq

\- gnbOnlyUserModifyAction is absent

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-36**  (ID: `12982587`)

DL HARQ Tx Modification of the DL MCS Table and/or PDSCH DMRS Type (responding to a L2-PS trigger)

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-36.0-2**  (ID: `12982640`)

DL HARQ Tx In response to a PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd (see [12789157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SEBVEJMUEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) CP-RT can send PsUser_UserModifyReq to start the reconfiguration of the DL MCS Table (qam64 from/to qam256, qam256 from/to qam1024 [CB008949-D], qam64 from/to qam1024 [End CB008949-D]) and/or of the PDSCH DMRS type.

If PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd requests the reconfiguration for both DL MCS table and PDSCH DMRS Type, CP-RT shall start the reconfiguration for both with the same PsUser_UserModifyReq.

At reception of such PsUser_UserModifyReq L2-PS shall:

  * stop timer rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer ([12789157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SEBVEJMUEfCoxNjZXyLbRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9));
  * Enter the transient phase ([1153814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksolSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9));



During the transient phase CP-RT can cancel the ongoing reconfiguration, by sending a second PsUser_UserModifyReq massage where:

  * the DL MCS Table reconfiguration is cancelled by setting PsUser_UserModifyReq.cellConfigurationForModification[0].pdschConfig.mcsTable = "cancelMcsTableReconfiguration";
  * the PDSCH DMRS Type reconfiguration is cancelled by setting PsUser_UserModifyReq.cellConfigurationForModification[0].pdschConfig.dmrsType = "cancelDmrsTypeReconfiguration";



If the reconfiguration is ongoing for both DL MCS table and PDSCH DMRS Type, a possible cancellation shall cancel both reconfigurations. No partial cancellation is supported.

At reception of PsUser_UserModifyReq to cancel the reconfiguration:

  * For the cancellation of the (qam64 from/to qam256, qam256 from/to qam1024 [CB008949-D], qam64 from/to qam1024 [End CB008949-D]) DL MCS Table reconfiguration, L2-PS shall take the same actions as for the cancellation of QAM64 from/to LowSE MCS Table reconfiguration ([11144973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_238pu_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) with the exclusion of the betaOffset rollback, which is relevant only when UL MCS Table is reconfigured and LowSE Table is involved.
  * For the cancellation of the PDSCH DMRS Type, L2-PS shall take the same actions as for the cancellation of (qam64 from/to qam256, qam256 from/to qam1024 [CB008949-D], qam64 from/to qam1024 [End CB008949-D]) DL MCS Table reconfiguration, but for the DMRS Type;
  * L2-PS shall restart the channel monitoring which was suspended after sending PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd;



After a cancellation no PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is sent.

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-37**  (ID: `13251170`)

DL HARQ Tx Sparse Sssg configuration handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-3.0-37.0-1**  (ID: `13251173`)

DL HARQ Tx CP-RT send PsUser_UserModifyReq for UE sparse SSSG configuration in two cases:

case1: UE sparse SSSG configuration setup(for sparseSSGroupIndex allocation), l2psRequiredIndTrigger is not present.

**[Before PR867429]**

case2: Response for L2-PS triggered SSSG Re-configuration, :

if l2psRequiredIndTrigger is sssgReconfiguration, and IE sparseSssgSwitchingConfig is present, L2-PS need wait RRC reconfiguration complete due to UE sparse SSSG configuration changed;

if l2psRequiredIndTrigger is sssgReconfiguration, and IE sparseSssgSwitchingConfig is NOT present, L2-PS update existed sparse SSSG configuration as valid.

Other handling refer to [12798424: User Reconfiguration required for sparse SSSG](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Hr064Jj2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

**[End PR867429]**

**[PR878479]**

case3:UE BWP reconfiguration.

When Cell BWP is switched to limited mode(refer to [12505866: Normal and limited bandwidth modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6-kc8RVSEfCV0v_Ffc8sJw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), all UEs will be reconfigured to limited BWP. The SSSG shall be reconfigured based on limited BWP's sparse configuration.

if sparseSssgSwitchingConfig it present, and cellBwpId is changed, L2-PS shall apply new SSSG for new active BWP, the UE will be start from Dense state after BWP reconfiguration complete. Refer to [11173767: UE SSSG Switching Configuration and Active Switching Algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26eZQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

**[End PR878479]**

---

##### 2.1.4.2.0-4 DL HARQ Tx Transmission of PsUser_UserModifyResp (ID: 11145041)

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11145048`)

DL HARQ Tx **More than one BWP configuration**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11145061`)

DL HARQ Tx If more than one BWP in PCell is configured for a UE in PsUser_UserModifyReq, L2PS shall generate a new dedicated TDRA list (see 5G_UP_ALG_6663_replaced([11115691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpw3dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and add this list to PsUser_UserModifyResp.

[CB008140-BB]

For inter-gNB CA PCell 5G-L2-PS shall send the PsUser_UserModifyResp message to PCell 5G-CP-RT without waiting for the PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message from SCell 5G-L2-PS.

[End CB008140-BB]

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11145072`)

DL HARQ Tx Uplink Configured Grant Type 2 Configuration handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145077`)

DL HARQ Tx Response handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11145088`)

DL HARQ Tx [Before CB008124-C]

When 5G L2-PS receives PsUser_UserModifyReq message with the structure "ulCgConfigType2" and the parameter "ulCgConfig" = 1 (CG Configuration) and csRnti allocation is done as in 5G_L2_9633_replaced([11144897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_238Cr_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DL scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserModifyResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok and parameter "csRnti" value.

UL Scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserModifyResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok or EStatus5G_NotOk and parameters "configuredGrantTimer" and "nrOfHarqProcesses".

EO SGNL verifies if status of both internal PsUser_UserModifyResp (from DL and UL scheduler) is EStatus5G_OK, and copies parameters "csRnti", "configuredGrantTimer" and "nrOfHarqProcesses" in the message PsUser_UserModifyResp that is send to CP-RT.

Note: If one of internal PsUser_UserModifyResp has status EStatus5G_NotOk, the csRnti remains allocated in UE databases until UE Release

[CB008124-C]

When 5G L2-PS receives PsUser_UserModifyReq message with the structure "ulCgConfigType2" and the parameter "ulCgConfig" = 1 (CG Configuration) and csRnti allocation is done as 5G_L2_9633_replaced([11144897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_238Cr_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DL scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserModifyResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti).

UL Scheduler sends internal PsUser_UserModifyResp to EO SGNL with status: EStatus5G_Ok and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer).

[Before PR700501]

EO SGNL verifies if status of both internal PsUser_UserModifyResp (from DL and UL scheduler) is EStatus5G_OK, and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer) in the message PsUser_UserModifyResp that is send to CP-RT.

[PR700501]

EO SGNL verifies if status of both internal PsUser_UserModifyResp (from DL and UL scheduler) is EStatus5G_OK, and ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer).

Then, Signalling EO will send an internal message to UL scheduler ("SgnlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd") that contains as information the csRnti and rnti value.

At reception of internal msg "SgnlToUlCsrntiAllocationInd" , UL scheduler store csRnti value in UE UL database

Then message PsUser_UserModifyResp that is send to CP-RT.

[End PR700501]

Note: If one of internal PsUser_UserModifyResp has status ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusNOK), the csRnti remains allocated in UE databases until UE Release

[End CB008124-C]

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between different components: UL Scheduler, DL Scheduler, SGNL, and CP-RT. The diagram uses colored boxes to represent the components and arrows to show the messages exchanged between them. Here's a breakdown of the diagram: **Components:** * **UL Scheduler (Green):** Represents the Uplink Scheduler. * **DL Scheduler (Blue):** Represents the Downlink Scheduler. * **SGNL (Yellow):** Represents a signaling component. * **CP-RT (Gray):** Represents a Control Plane - Real-Time component. **Messages and Actions:** 1\. **UL Scheduler to SGNL:** * `UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: The UL Scheduler sends a request to SGNL to modify user configuration. 2\. **DL Scheduler to UL Scheduler:** * `internal:: UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: The DL Scheduler sends an internal request to the UL Scheduler with user configuration details. 3\. **csRntiAllocator (within DL Scheduler's scope):** * `Store in DL UE db: csRnti`: This indicates that a `csRnti` (Cell Radio Network Temporary Identifier) is stored in the DL UE database. 4\. **UL Scheduler to DL Scheduler:** * `internal:: UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: The UL Scheduler sends an internal request to the DL Scheduler with user configuration details. 5\. **Actions within UL Scheduler's scope:** * `Store in UL UE db:`: Indicates storage in the UL UE database. * `ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile`: These parameters are stored. * `API dB Cell: getCgTimerAndNrOfHarqProcessPair`: An API call to get timer and HARQ process information. 6\. **DL Scheduler to UL Scheduler:** * `internal::UserModifyResp(Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK,csRnti))`: The DL Scheduler responds to the UL Scheduler with a success message and allocation results, including `csRnti`. 7\. **UL Scheduler to DL Scheduler:** * `internal::UserModifyResp (Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer))`: The UL Scheduler responds to the DL Scheduler with a success message and allocation results, including HARQ process count and grant timer. 8\. **SGNL's actions:** * `SGNL check resp from both schedulers`: SGNL verifies the responses from both the UL and DL Schedulers. * `and if it's ok send SgnlToUICsrntiAllocationInd, update and send the UserSetupResp to CP-RT`: If the responses are satisfactory, SGNL sends an indication to the UL Scheduler and updates and sends a response to CP-RT. 9\. **SGNL to UL Scheduler:** * `internal::SgnlToUICsrntiAllocationInd(rnti, csRnti)`: SGNL sends an indication to the UL Scheduler about `csRnti` allocation. 10\. **Actions within UL Scheduler's scope (after receiving from SGNL):** * `Store in UL UE db:`: Indicates storage in the UL UE database. * `csRnti received from SGNL`: Notes the reception of `csRnti` from SGNL. * `csRnti allocated in DL sched`: Indicates that `csRnti` has been allocated in the DL scheduler. 11\. **SGNL to CP-RT:** * `UserModifyResp (OK, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK, csRnti, nbOfHarqProcesses, configuredGrantTimer))`: SGNL sends a modified user response to CP-RT, including allocation status, `csRnti`, HARQ process count, and grant timer.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_694.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145093`)

DL HARQ Tx Exception handling: csRnti Allocation Failure

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145104`)

DL HARQ Tx Exception: csRnti Allocation Failure

L2PS DL scheduler shall consider all the available rnti pools, if the total number of remaining available RNTIs, in percentage, is less than or equal to rdCgMinRntiAvailability (see 5G_UP_ALG_15495_replaced([11173568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuUnUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), CS-RNTI allocation shall be considered as not successful.

L2PS signalling should send UserModifyResp including status: EStatus5G_Ok and ulCgType2AllocationResult structure ( 5G_L2_IF_4389_replaced([10976545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLwvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

> CgAllocationStatus CgAllocationStatusNOK
> 
> CgAllocationCause lackOfCsRnti

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between different components, likely in a telecommunications system. The diagram uses colored boxes to represent different entities and arrows to show the messages exchanged between them. Here's a breakdown of the components and interactions: **Entities:** * **UL Scheduler (Green):** Represents the Uplink Scheduler. * **DL Scheduler (Blue):** Represents the Downlink Scheduler. * **csRntiAllocator (Blue):** Represents a component responsible for allocating CS-RNTI (Cell-Specific Radio Network Temporary Identifier). * **SGML (Yellow):** Likely a signaling or management entity. * **CP-RT (Gray):** Likely a Control Plane Real-Time component. * **Store in UL JE db (Green):** Represents a data storage or database operation for the UL JE (Uplink Joint Encoding) component. **Interactions (Messages):** 1\. **UL Scheduler to DL Scheduler:** * `internal::UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: An internal request to modify configuration, including UL CG (Carrier Group) configuration, MCS table, and UL CG profile. 2\. **DL Scheduler to csRntiAllocator:** * `internal::UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: Similar to the above, an internal request to modify configuration. * **Comment:** "Should check rdCgMinRntiAvailability" - This indicates a check for the availability of a minimum RNTI. 3\. **csRntiAllocator to SGML:** * `UserModifyReq(ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile)`: A request to modify configuration sent to SGML. 4\. **Store in UL JE db:** * **Data Stored:** `ulCgConfig, ulCgMcsTable, ulCgProfile` * **API Call:** `API dB Cell: getCgTimerAndNrOfHarqProcessPair` \- An API call to retrieve CG timer and number of HARQ processes. 5\. **DL Scheduler to UL Scheduler:** * `internal::UserModifyResp (Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult(CgAllocationStatusNOK, lackOfCsRnti))`: An internal response indicating success ("Ok") but with a failure in UL CG Type 2 Allocation, specifically a "NOK" (Not OK) status and a "lackOfCsRnti". 6\. **UL Scheduler to SGML:** * `internal::UserModifyResp(Ok, ulCgType2AllocationResult (CgAllocationStatusOK, nbOfHarq Processes, configuredGrantTimer))`: An internal response indicating success ("Ok") with a successful UL CG Type 2 Allocation, including the number of HARQ processes and the configured grant timer. 7\. **SGML:** * **Comment:** "SGNL check resp from both schedulers and include ulCgType2AllocationResult for cs-Rnti allocation failure" - This indicates SGML's role in verifying responses from both schedulers and incorporating the UL CG Type 2 Allocation result, especially in cases of CS-RNTI allocation failure. 8\. **SGML to CP-RT:** * `UserModifyResp (OK, ulCgType2AllocationResult(CgAllocationStatusNOK, lackOfCsRnti))`: A response to CP-RT indicating success ("OK") but with a failure in UL CG Type 2 Allocation, specifically a "NOK" status and a "lackOfCsRnti". **2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11145111`)

DL HARQ Tx CG Config failure detected in L2PS UL Scheduler

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11145117`)

DL HARQ Tx CG Config failure detected in UL Scheduler

L2PS UL Scheduler shall consider the UL TransformPrecoder state. if this state is different from DISABLED, UE cannot be CG Configured and PsUser_ModifyReq is rejected.

L2PS signalling shall send UserModifyResp including status: EStatus5G_NOk with Cause InvalidParameter

an including ulCgType2AllocationResult structure ( 5G_L2_IF_4389_replaced([10976545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLwvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

> CgAllocationStatus CgAllocationStatusNOK
> 
> CgAllocationCause other

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11145123`)

DL HARQ Tx Uplink Configured Grant Type 2 Configuration Rollback handling

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11145130`)

DL HARQ Tx When 5G L2-PS receives a PsUser_UserModifyReq message with the structure "ulCgConfigType2" and the parameter "ulCgConfig" = 2 (CG configuration cancelation) (see 5G_L2_IF_4008_replaced([10976380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VF9q_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2PS shall release CG state machine (refer to 5G_L2_9679_replaced([11176112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26xUOfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L2PS signalling should send UserModifyResp satus: EStatus5G_OK including ulCgType2AllocationResult structure ( 5G_L2_IF_4389_replaced([10976545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLwvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

> CgAllocationStatus CgAllocationStatusOK

and in case of failure:

> CgAllocationStatus CgAllocationStatusNOK
> 
> CgAllocationCause Other

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11145137`)

DL HARQ Tx **UL Tx Switching PUSCH dedicated TDRA handling**

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `13336474`)

DL HARQ Tx In User Modify procedure for TDD UL Tx switching SCell addition and release or step-wise SCell addition to CA UE [CB010741-C] or SCell Upgrade from DL to DL_UL [CB010741-C] accompanied with PCell/reatained SCell UL TX switching **reconfiguration, FDD Pcell or SCell UL scheduler shall generate a new dedicated TDRA list (see 5G_UP_ALG_24789_replaced([11115992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or**[11204898: Dedicate entry for FDD + TDD FR1 UL Tx Switching in FDD PCell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4PPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA) [End CB014465-B] ) and if the new generated TDRA list introduce new element **add this list to PsUser_UserModifyResp. DCI Format 0_0 and 0_1 conflict detection is needed (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

For TDD UL Tx switching SCell addition **or ulTxSwitch is configured from 'disable' to other than 'disable' on FDD serving cell:**

If NRCELL.actUlSlotAgg = TRUE on FDD PCell and the UE is not eligible for Slot Aggregation (see 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as NRCELL.actUlSlotAgg = FALSE:

puschTimeDomainAllocationList IE shall be updated according to [11115992: Dedicate entry for FR1 UL Tx Switching in FDD Cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

else if NRCELL.actUlSlotAgg = TRUE on FDD PCell and the UE is eligible for Slot Aggregation (see 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

puschTimeDomainAllocationListR16 IE shall be updated according to [11204898: Dedicate entry for FDD + TDD FR1 UL Tx Switching in FDD PCell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4PPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)

endif

For TDD UL Tx switching SCell release:

On FDD PCell, the update in puschTimeDomainAllocationList or puschTimeDomainAllocationListR16 for UL TX Switch shall be rolled back.

FDD Pcell **or SCell UL scheduler shall start transient phase as per 5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and finish transient phase if PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is received** or upon the completion of DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion (5G_UP_ALG_29060_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Transient phase handling for FR1 FDD + TDD UL TX switch option1 UE shall follow 5G_L2_16809_replaced([11160989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25YNHPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**During transient phase of PCell, L2-PS shall also follow the DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure specified by 5G_L2_22365_replaced([11170588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26K3TfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `11145163`)

DL HARQ Tx Delay PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP-RT then transient phase

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11145178`)

DL HARQ Tx When dmrsAdditionalPosition is reconfigured by PsUser_UserModifyReq as 5G_L2_18559_replaced([11144838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_238CpvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if the reconfigured UE is DL CA UE with at least one activated SCell, then the PsUser_UserModifyResp should be delayed, sending to CP-RT until possible allocated pucch in DPA for this UE is used up. And after sending PsUser_UserModifyResp to CP-RT, the user should enter transient phase to be scheduled only by DCI1_0 in PCell and DPA stops even if UE is CA UE.

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-6**  (ID: `12762759`)

DL HARQ Tx DCI format 0_1 and 0_0 size conflict and TDRA list modification

---

**2.1.4.2.0-4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12762725`)

DL HARQ Tx L2-PS shall check the DCI format 0_0 and 0_1 size, and modify the TDRA list if the size of the 2 formats are equal, as defined in [(11171658: DCI Format 0_0 and 0_1 conflict detection and TDRA list modification](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). If the TDRA list is updated, the list is sent to CP-RT in the psUser_UserModifyResp via the parameter puschTimeDomainAllocationList.

[(](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_r_TT4PvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)[11170549: Transient phase for the UE with a dedicated configuration (with an explicit state of UE dedicated configuration)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26K3RPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) defines that some of new configurations present in psUser_UserModifyReq are not immediately taken into account, they are temporary saved as pending configuration as long as the UE does not confirmed the reception of the RRC-RECONF, L2-PS shall however use the new Aperiodic CSI configuration and the new number of dedicated Bandwidth Parts coming from psUser_UserModifyReq to calculate the size of the DCI format 0_1.

---

### 2.1.4.3 User Stop Scheduling

#### 2.1.4.3.0-2 User Stop Scheduling Reception of PsUser_UserStopReq (ID: 11145197)

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145204`)

User Stop Scheduling Evaluation of IE cause

---

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11145209`)

User Stop Scheduling cause = handover

---

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11145216`)

User Stop Scheduling When 5G-L2-PS receives valid PsUser_UserStopReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_2569_replaced([10976632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHy0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with the cause IE set to handover, then it shall:

• stop UE scheduling;

• trigger update relevant PM counter from Serving Beam ID before HO group (M55305C02001- M55305C02064);

• send PsUser_UserStopResp (see 5G_L2_IF_2554_replaced([10976684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHy2vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to 5G-CP-RT.

---

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11145223`)

User Stop Scheduling cause = release

---

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145233`)

User Stop Scheduling When 5G-L2-PS instance receives PsUser_UserStopReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_459_replaced([10976556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with the cause IE set to release, then the instance shall:

In [CB008294-A]FR1[End CB008294-A] SA CA:

• stop UE scheduling on target SCell(s) listed in ScellToStopList IE;

• send PsUser_UserStopResp to 5G-CP-RT.

[CB008294-A]In FR2 SA CA:

• stop UE scheduling in PCell and SCell(s);

• in UE context set the parameter isUserStopReceived toTrue, to indicate the successful reception of PsUser_UserStopReq;

• send PsUser_UserStopResp to 5G-CP-RT.[End CB008294-A]

In [CB008294-A]FR1/FR2[End CB008294-A] NSA CA:

• stop UE scheduling on target SCell(s) listed in remoteScellToStopList IE;

• send PsUser_UserStopResp to 5G-CP-RT.

In [CB008294-A]FR1/FR2[End CB008294-A] SA/NSA non-CA:

• stop UE scheduling on actual (nrCellIdentity IE) cell;

• send PsUser_UserStopResp to 5G-CP-RT.

Note: See 5G_L3_5369_replaced([11062015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BCkx4P_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)) and 5G_L2_IF_459_replaced([10976556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more info.

---

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11145241`)

**2.1.4.3.0-2.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11145247`)

### 2.1.4.4 User Delete

#### 2.1.4.4.0-2 User Delete Reception of PsUser_UserDeleteReq (ID: 11145302)

**2.1.4.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145314`)

User Delete In FR2 SA CA, when 5G-L2-PS instance receives PsUser_UserDeleteReq (see 5G_L2_IF_467_replaced([10976708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHy4Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the instance shall:

[Before CNI-120470]

 send PsUser_UserDeleteResp (see 5G_L2_IF_5366_replaced([10976812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VIZ7vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 check in the UE context value of isUserStopReceived (see 5G_L2_8356_replaced([11145223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23933_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if it is equal to False (5G-L2-PS did not received successfully the PsUser_UserStopReq for this UE, see 5G_L2_IF_459_replaced([10976556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS shall stop UE scheduling in PCell and SCell(s);

 delete UE context common for PCell and SCell(s);

[CNI-120470]

  * check in the UE context value of isUserStopReceived (see 5G_L2_8356_replaced([11145223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23933_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if it is equal to False (5G-L2-PS did not received successfully the PsUser_UserStopReq for this UE, see 5G_L2_IF_459_replaced([10976556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHLxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS shall stop UE scheduling in PCell and SCell(s);



 delete UE context common for PCell and SCell(s);

 send PsUser_UserDeleteResp (see 5G_L2_IF_5366_replaced([10976812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VIZ7vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CNI-120470]

#### 2.1.4.4.0-3 User Delete C-RNTI release in ext-SCell (ID: 11145320)

**2.1.4.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11145332`)

User Delete [Before CB008140-I-UPD008]

When 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserDeleteReq message during ext-SCell release procedure (see 5G_L3_FLOW_65978) or UE context release procedure in ext-gNB (see 5G_L3_FLOW_58175), the ext-L2-PS shall release the C-RNTI reserved during the ext-SCell addition procedure (see 5G_L2_140_replaced([11143950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233KKPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by pushing it back to the list of free C-RNTIs (see 5G_UP_ALG_3403_replaced([11152041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and follow the C-RNTI cooling down protection algorithm (see 5G_L2_680_replaced([11170288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26IbDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
[CB008140-I-UPD008]

When 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserDeleteReq message during (ext-)SCell release procedure (see 5G_L3_FLOW_65978) or UE context release procedure in ext-gNB (see 5G_L3_FLOW_58175), the L2-PS in (ext-)Scell shall release the C-RNTI reserved during the (ext-)SCell addition procedure (see 5G_L2_140_replaced([11143950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233KKPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by unreserve C-RNTI in cell and push back C-RNTI to list of free C-RNTis (see 5G_UP_ALG_3403_replaced([11152041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only when during (ext-)SCell addition procedure C-RNTI was removed from the list of free C-RNTIs and follow the C-RNTI cooling down protection algorithm (see 5G_L2_680_replaced([11170288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26IbDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  
[End CB008140-I-UPD008]

#### 2.1.4.4.0-4 User Delete List of unconfigured slices (ID: 11145339)

**2.1.4.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11145353`)

User Delete [Before CB008828-C]

Upon reception of the PsUser_UserDeleteReq L2-PS shall update list of unconfigured slices (see 5G_L2_11072_replaced([11176812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_262zyfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with following rules:

\- sum of schedule weight should be decreased for every slice that is associated to DRB from PsUser_UserDeleteReq

\- every slice without any DRB association should be removed.

[End CB008828-C]

---

#### 2.1.4.4.0-5 User Delete Checking status of currently ongoing user deletions (ID: 13343451)

**2.1.4.4.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13368304`)

User Delete [05080575]

~~When a new procedure (f.e user delete) is added, this mechanism checks the status of currently ongoing procedures.  
If 6 HFN (approximately 1 minute) has passed since the last check, the queue of ongoing (unfinished) procedures is then inspected.  
If any procedure has been running for more than 6 HFN (approximately 1 minute), It is removed from the queue.~~

Periodic procedure of checking ongoing (unfinished) procedures (f.e user delete) is removed. Instead of it, L2PS synchronizes procedures between its subcomponents (downlink and uplink schedulers) so that unfinished procedures are finalized and completed correctly and not interrupted midway by newly called procedures.

[End 05080575]

---

Bulk User Request When 5G-L2-PS receives valid PsUser_BulkUserReq message L2-PS shall stop scheduling of all the UEs [CNI-113978] listed in associatedUeList[] or stop scheduling of all the UEs of the specified cell if associatedUeList[] is empty [End CNI-113978] in the cell specified in the nrCellIdentity.

[CNI-113978] If associatedUeList[] is not empty, Scheduling of UEs not listed in associatedUeList[numOfUe] IE shall not be affected. [End CNI-113978]

**2.1.4.5.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145422`)

[End CNI-113978]

### 2.1.4.8 Radio Bearer Setup

#### 2.1.4.8.0-2 Radio Bearer Setup Reception of PsUser_BearerSetupReq (ID: 11145584)

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145591`)

Radio Bearer Setup TTI tracing

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12786923`)

Radio Bearer Setup dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr

If first HR DRB bearer is being set up for a user by PsUser_BearerSetupReq and MCS table in PDSCH is not configured to 256QAM[CB008949-C] or 1024QAM [End CB008949-C] and ulCgMcsTable is not configured to 256QAM and 5QI-1/65/66 DRB is not set up, L2-PS DL scheduler shall trace TTI trace item dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11227_replaced([11205736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to dlFirstHrDrbSetup and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

If UE become ineligible for HR LA mode due to ulCgMcsTable configured with 256QAM, then L2-PS DL scheduler shall trace TTI trace item dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11227_replaced([11205736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to configuredGrantWithQam256Setup and the LA mode as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_15603_replaced([11125162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) will be applicable afterwards.

When 5QI-1/65/66 DRB is setup while UE operates in HR LA mode, then the L2-PS DL scheduler shall switch the UE to BR LA mode and trace TTI trace item dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11227_replaced([11205736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to vonrBearerSetup and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

ulLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr

Similarly, if MCS table in PUSCH is not configured to 256QAM and 5QI-1/65/66 DRB is not set up**, L2-PS UL scheduler shall trace ulLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11231_replaced([11205767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with ulFirstHrDrbSetup and new LA mode.**

When 5QI-1/65/66 DRB is setup while UE operates in HR LA mode, then the L2-PS UL scheduler shall switch the UE to BR LA mode and trace TTI trace item ulLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11231_replaced([11205767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to voNrBearerSetup and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145611`)

Radio Bearer Setup DRB to slice association

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11145635`)

Radio Bearer Setup [Before CB008828-C]

For all structures within drbAddReqPs list field of PsUser_BearerSetupReq message (received from CP-RT) L2-PS shall store information about DRB to slice association (snssai structure) if available, regardless of slice awareness has been configured or not for both configured and unconfigured slices (For further details refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17581_replaced([11188712](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvd22_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_11072_replaced([11176812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_262zyfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If DRB is associated to the slice that don’t exist on configured or unconfigured slice list, L2PS should add that slice to the list of unconfigured slices.

This information is needed in case slice aware scheduler activation flag (sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation under PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq, see 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or slice list (plmnConfigList under PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq, see 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is modified as an on-line change.

If actNsaResourceGroupSlicing is enabled:

L2-PS shall store the information about DRB to NSA resource group association ([Before CNI-116869]resourceGroupId[CNI-116869]dl/ulResourceGroupId[End CNI-116869] parameter) if available. If neither snssai nor resourceGroupId is present within drbAddReqPs, L2-PS shall assume DRB belongs to NSA resource group default for user's PLMN. In that case, L2-PS shall resolve the DRB to NSA resource group association on an as-needed basis in runtime using nsaDefaultResourceGroupId (see 5G_L2_IF_1665_replaced([10969775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ue5ovu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: In context of Slice Aware Scheduler, NSA resource group is referred to as a "slice", see 5G_UP_ALG_7387_replaced([11188675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvd21PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008828-C]

L2-PS should map bearer to the resource group according to 5G_UP_ALG_19736_replaced([11188754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB008709-A](DL), 5G_UP_ALG_23406_replaced([11206779](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwr-1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL) [End CB008709-A].

[End CB008828-C]

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11145642`)

Radio Bearer Setup Configuration of DRB-specific maximum number of HARQ transmissions

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11145649`)

Radio Bearer Setup For each entry of the drbAddReqPs list field (please see 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received in PsUser_BearerSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall store information about optionally configured DRB-specific maximum number of HARQ transmissions for both DL (maxDlHarqTxDrb) and UL (maxUlHarqTxDrb) and use them as input for procedures described in 5G_UP_ALG_12742_replaced([11185319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvSQpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively.

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11145654`)

Radio Bearer Setup Partial addition of DRBs in ext-gNB

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11145661`)

Radio Bearer Setup If PsUser_BearerSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_496_replaced([10977222](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VLdMvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message is received in ext-gNB during Inter gNB CA, 5G-L2-PS shall process each entry of drbAddReqPs list (5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) independently.

For each failed DRB addition 5G-L2-PS shall add entry to drbFailToAddList list (in PsUser_BearerSetupResp, see 5G_L2_IF_497_replaced([10977256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VLdN_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) containing:

\- logicalChannelIdentity of DRB that could not be added

\- cause of DRB addition failure

If at least one DRB addition succeeds, 5G-L2-PS shall send PsUser_BearerSetupResp with status EStatus5G_Ok. Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall send PsUser_BearerSetupResp with status EStatus5G_NotOk and cause ECause5G_Undefined.

Radio Bearer Setup Addition of HR DRB bearer

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12786931`)

Note 2: If PUSCH is configured with 256QAM table then HR DRB bearer(s) are successfully added but continues to operate in BR LA for uplink transmissions until PUSCH is reconfigured to either 64QAM/64QAM LowSE.

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11145679`)

Radio Bearer Setup Handling of NBR parameters

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12463109`)

Radio Bearer Setup 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_BearerSetupReq message with structure "drbAddReqPs" and if this structure in turn contains structure [Before CB008118-B] "nbrDrbSpecificParams" [CB008118-B] nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams [End CB008118], then the parameters present in structure [Before CB008118-B] "nbrDrbSpecificParams" [CB008118-B] nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams [End CB008118] are stored in ue context. For details of parameters to be stored refer to 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

NBR Congestion Control Priority parameters shall not be present in the nbrDrbSpecificParams received by L2-PS when NBR Congestion control is in deactivated state. L2-PS shall store default values for priority (as defined in 5G_L2_17206_replaced([11177154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_265QCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UE context . The default priority values shall be used for existing UE's / bearer when NBR Congestion control is dynamically enabled and unless the priority is modifed by a separate procedure.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0 (Spare value) , the priority shall be initialized to the default of 14.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 15 (No Priority), the priority value 15 shall be treated lower than the lowest priotiy level (14) for NBR Congestion Control.

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `12463115`)

Radio Bearer Setup Handling of GBR Congestion control Parameters

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12463118`)

Radio Bearer Setup 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_BearerSetupReq message with structure "drbAddReqPs" and if this structure in turn contains structure nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams, then the parameters present in structure nbrGbrDrbSpecificParams are stored in ue context. For details of parameters to be stored refer to 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

GBR Congestion Control Priority parameters shall not be present in the DRB configuration parameter received by L2-PS when GBR Congestion control is in deactivated state. L2-PS shall store default values for priority (as defined in 5G_L2_397_replaced([11151857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24k72fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UE context . The default priority values shall be used for existing UE's / bearer when GBR Congestion control is dynamically enabled and unless the priority is modifed by a separate procedure.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0 (Spare value) , the priority shall be initialized to the default of 14.

Note: If value of priorityLevelArp (in 5G_L2_IF_397_replaced([10974876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-o4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 15 (No Priority), the priority value 15 shall be treated lower than the lowest priotiy level (14) for GBR Congestion Control.

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11145699`)

Radio Bearer Setup Check static UE when DRB setup

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11145705`)

Radio Bearer Setup Check whether UE is static UE as 5G_L2_22155_replaced([11144207](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YTPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when UE's DRB is increased by PsUser_BearerSetupReq. If the reducing PCSI processing is enabled as 5G_UP_ALG_29643_replaced([11159287](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktIUjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and UE's static UE status is changed as 5G_UP_ALG_29639_replaced([11159298](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktIUj_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the TA Grant timer should be changed as 5G_UP_ALG_4845_replaced([11195726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv-NIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Radio Bearer Setup DRB priority Proactive Uplink Grant configuration or re-configuration

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11145719`)

Radio Bearer Setup L2-PS shall configure or re-configure DRB priority PUG and store or update DRB priority PUG profile on UE level for later usage according to 5G_L2_23568_replaced([11151708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24kUwPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `13397718`)

Radio Bearer Setup Critical bearer setup

---

**2.1.4.8.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `13397719`)

Radio Bearer Setup L2-PS shall check the criticality of the bearers requested for setup as mentioned below

  1. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and SRBs part of PsUser_BearerSetupReq-> srbAddReqPs[] have their criticalSrbSchedEnabled = True, those respective SRBs are marked as critical SRBs. L2-PS also shall check the DRB criticality to decide the SRB criticality as mentioned in the next steps.



2\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_BearerSetupReq-> drbAddReqPs[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as critical DRBs and SRBs.

3\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_BearerSetupReq-> drbAddReqPs[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = False, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

4\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = False and SRBs or DRBs part of PsUser_BearerSetupReq have their criticality flags criticalSrbSchedEnabled = True or criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, L2-PS shall print a warning message and consider them as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

Note : SRB criticality is decide in three phases.

Phase1 : When there is no DRB. In this phase SRB criticality is decided by its flag criticalSrbSchedEnabled.

Phase2 : When a DRB is setup, SRB criticality is decided by the DRB such that if one or more DRBs are marked with criticalDrbSchedEnabled = true, then the mapping SRB is also considered critical irrespective of its criticalSrbSchedEnabled status.

Phase3: When the last DRB is removed, SRB is considered non critical

---

### 2.1.4.9 Radio Bearer Delete

#### 2.1.4.9.0-2 Radio Bearer Delete Reception of PsUser_BearerDeleteReq (ID: 11145740)

**2.1.4.9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145745`)

Radio Bearer Delete TTI tracing

---

**2.1.4.9.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11145758`)

Radio Bearer Delete If last HR DRB bearer is being deleted for a user by PsUser_BearerDeleteReq and 5QI-1[CB008118-CB]/65/66[End CB008118-CB] DRB is not set up, L2-PS DL scheduler shall trace TTI trace item dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11227_replaced([11205736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to dlLastHrDrbReleased and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

When 5QI-1[CB008118-CB]/65/66[End CB008118-CB] DRB is removed, UE’s eligibility for LA is evaluated as per 5G_UP_ALG_15603_replaced([11125162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If LA mode is switched to HR LA mode, then the L2-PS DL scheduler shall trace TTI trace item dlLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11227_replaced([11205736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to voNrBearerReleased and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

Similarly L2-PS UL scheduler shall trace ulLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11231_replaced([11205767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with ulLastHrDrbReleased and new LA mode when 5QI-1[CB008118-CB]/65/66[End CB008118-CB] DRB is not set up.

When 5QI-1[CB008118-CB]/65/66[End CB008118-CB] DRB is removed, UE’s eligibility for LA is evaluated as per 5G_UP_ALG_15603_replaced([11125162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If LA mode is swiched to HR LA mode, then the L2-PS UL scheduler shall trace TTI trace item ulLaSwitchBetweenHrAndBr (5G_L2_11231_replaced([11205767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-HjKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with event field set to voNrBearerReleased and the new LA mode applicable afterwards.

---

Radio Bearer Delete Check static UE when DRB delete

### 2.1.4.12 Random Access Indication

#### 2.1.4.12.0-2 Random Access Indication Handling RA Idications for muted beams (ID: 11145840)

**2.1.4.12.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12828385`)

Random Access Indication Upon reception of the UlData_PrachReceiveInd from L1 corresponding to the cell for which some SSB beams are muted [PR852424] or not available according to inactiveSsbFR2 setting [End PR852424], each detected preamble corresponding to the muted SSB beam (according to 5G_UP_ALG_2237_replaced([11113810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpd8j_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR852424] or corresponding to the unavailable SSB beam (according to [11111484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End PR852424] shall be ignored.

**Note 1: Correspondence of the detected preamble to the beam is implied by cell configuration and can be verified based on the fields slot of the UlData_PrachReceiveInd, and prachPreambleTimeOccasion and prachPreambleFreqOccasion of appropriate entry in the message.**

**Note 2: Meaning of the “ignore” in the requirement is as follows: no UE context is created as a result of reception of the preamble and procedures for sending Msg2 are not triggered (see also apprpriate flows under 5G_L1L2_FLOW_177_replaced([11186242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be_oQ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

#### 2.1.4.12.0-3 Random Access Indication Filtering RA indication when UE is far from gNB antenna (ID: 13314415)

**2.1.4.12.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13314447`)

Random Access Indication Filtering RA indication message: 

When a UE is far from gNB Antenna, the initialTa value in Rach Ind Message is high.

if actRachTaFilt activation flag is true and if initialTa is greater or equal to taDiscThreshold, then the Rach ind message is ignored by 5G-L2-PS.

where:  
\- actRachTaFilt and taDiscThreshold are received by 5G-L2-PS in cellSetupReq and cellReconfigurationReq message.  
\- initialTa value is received by 5G-L2-PS in PrachReceiveInd sent by L1.

Refer to [11152587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kshQgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

### 2.1.4.13 Radio Link Status Indication

#### 2.1.4.13.0-2 Radio Link Status Indication Indication of UL bad Radio Conditions (ID: 11145865)

**2.1.4.13.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145878`)

Radio Link Status Indication L2-PS shall send PsUser_RadioLinkStatusInd with ueRlStatus = 'bad_ul_radio' to notify CP-RT of detected bad UL radio conditions for the UE on the Pcell (SA call only). The different mechanisms which can trigger this indication are specified in 5G_UP_ALG_24965_replaced([11208582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwvCKfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Only up to one notification per call is sent. [PR741832] No notification is sent if the UE scheduling has been stopped (5G_UP_ALG_4823_replaced([11194949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4tkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or suspended (5G_UP_ALG_4831_replaced([11195211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6ixfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End PR741832]

### 2.1.4.14 Beam Group Change Indication

#### 2.1.4.14.0-1 Beam Group Change Indication FA: Beamforming/MIMO​ Document Owner: Michael 1. Wang (NSB); Michal Fiejka (Nokia) (ID: 11145891)

### 2.1.4.15 User Reconfiguration Required

#### 2.1.4.15.0-2 User Reconfiguration Required User reconfiguration required for No Additional DL Dmrs switch (ID: 11145910)

**2.1.4.15.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145921`)

User Reconfiguration Required No Addtional Dl Dmrs Switch is the algorithm as 5G_UP_ALG_27186_replaced([11157630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks8uV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When a UE is triggered for No Additional Dl Dmrs configuration as 5G_UP_ALG_27248_replaced([11157672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and UE is not in the procedure of "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration procedure triggered by itself, should send PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = config, a DL SDMRS reonfiguration procedure starts.

When a UE is triggered for No Additional Dl Dmrs release as 5G_UP_ALG_27212_replaced([11157682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks9VYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and UE is not in the procedure of "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration triggered by itself, should send PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = release, a DL DMRS reonfiguration procedure starts.

UE is not in the procedure of "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration triggered by itself, means that the reconfiguration procedure is done in any of the bellow case:

1\. UE has never triggerred a PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = config/release;

2\. If UE has triggered PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = config/release, PsUser_UserModifyReq from CP modifies Dl Dmrs as PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd required, and PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq is received so the reconfiguration procedure is done;

3\. If UE has triggered PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = config/release, a PsUser_UserModifyReq with [Before CNI-107035]isCancellation = TRUE[CNI-107035]cancellationType is tasSrsOrNoAddDlDmrs[End CNI-107035] for the reconfiguration reqirement, the procedure is done;

4\. If UE has triggered PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = config and then no response from CP is received on Dl Dmrs configuration(no PsUser_UserModifyReq message or PsUser_UserModifyReq from CP does not modify Dl Dmrs), and rrmNoAddDlDmrsConfigProhibitTimer is time out, the reconfiguration procedure is done;

5\. If UE has triggered PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to CP with IE noAddDlDmrsInd = release and then no response from CP is received on Dl Dmrs configuration(no PsUser_UserModifyReq message or PsUser_UserModifyReq from CP does not modify Dl Dmrs), and rrmNoAddDlDmrsRealeseProhibitTimer is time out, the reconfiguration procedure is done.

If UE is triggered the procedure of 2,3,4,5 but not done yet, PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd with IE tasSrsResourceInd = subband for SB BF release can't be sent to CP.

---

#### 2.1.4.15.0-3 User Reconfiguration Required User reconfiguration required for tasSrsResource (ID: 11145928)

**2.1.4.15.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11145936`)

User Reconfiguration Required Trigger for changing from SB SRS to WB SRS

---

**2.1.4.15.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13457039`)

User Reconfiguration Required 1.When L2-PS send PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd, start a ReconfigRequiredInd timer(defined by rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer) for WB SRS switch

2.If rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer is expires, L2 Ps set the UE back to SB SRS state.

3.If PsUser_UserModifyReq->bwpConfig**.**[Before CB015122-A]isWBTasConfigured**[CB015122-A]isTasSrsForSubbandBmConfigured**[End CB015122-A] = True, L2 Ps shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**_*_** *

4.If CP-RT indicates that the RRC Reconfiguration has been completed succesfully (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq->tasSrsResourceInd= success) L2 Ps shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else if CP-RT request to cancel the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->cancellationType is tasSrsOrNoAddDlDmrs),L2 Ps shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**2.1.4.15.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11145948`)

User Reconfiguration Required Trigger for changing from SB WB SRS to SB SRS

---

**2.1.4.15.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13457056`)

User Reconfiguration Required 1.When L2-PS send PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd, start a ReconfigRequiredInd timer(defined by rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer) for SB SRS switch

2.If rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer is expires, 5G-L2-PS set the UE back to WB SRS state.

3.If PsUser_UserModifyReq->bwpConfig.**[Before CB015122-A]isWBTasConfigured**[CB015122-A]isTasSrsForSubbandBmConfigured**[End CB015122-A] = False, 5G-L2-PS shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))******

4.If CP-RT indicates that the RRC Reconfiguration has been completed succesfully (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq->tasSrsResourceInd= success) 5G-L2-PS shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else if CP-RT request to cancel the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->cancellationType is tasSrsOrNoAddDlDmrs), 5G-L2-PS shall take action refer to 5G_L2_12997_replaced([11171221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26MsevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

#### 2.1.4.15.0-4 User Reconfiguration Required User Reconfiguration required for DL MCS Table and/or PDSCH DMRS Type (ID: 12789157)

**2.1.4.15.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12877916`)

User Reconfiguration Required If

  * NRCELL.actDlMcsTableAndDmrsSwitching != DISABLED for a given UE Context, or
  * [Before CB008949-D] dl1024QamDynamicSwitch is TRUE ([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and [End CB008949-D] pdschSupConfig.pdsch1024QamFr1 is set to TRUE ([10975032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_P9Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))



L2-PS can request the reconfiguration of the DL MCS Table (qam64 from/to qam256, qam256 from/to qam1024 [CB008949-D] , qam64 from/to qam1024 [End CB008949-D] and/or PDSCH DMRS Type1 from/to Type2.

If the condition to trigger the MCS Table reconfiguration ([11129283](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq7VHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and the condition to trigger the DMRS Type Reconfiguration ([12483265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pPSrwA-UEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) are realized in the same slot:

  * the request to reconfigure both is sent in the same PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd message by setting the corresponding IEs dlMcsTableChangeInd and dlDmrsTypeChangeInd.



If the condition to trigger the DMRS Type re-configurations is realized after that a request to re-configure the DL MCS table is issued by L2-PS (or vice-versa, depending on the NIDD thresholds values):

  * L2-PS buffers the second requests and sends it after the reconfiguration related to the first request is either rejected (see below) or cancelled ([12982587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SSeeEbnzEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) or completed (PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq received)



After PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd transmission L2-PS:

  * Shall stop the channel monitoring described in [11129283](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq7VHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), if PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd.dlMcsTableChangeInd != NotApplicable
  * Shall stop the channel monitoring described in [12483265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pPSrwA-UEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), if PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd.dlDmrsTypeChangeInd != NotApplicable
  * shall start a timer which length is defined by rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer (see [11186656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277Kx_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). Reason: If such request is rejected by CP-RT (for example because another RRC reconfiguration is ongoing), CP-RT discards PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd without further notification to L2-PS (see [10994581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_76_u2Pu9Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).



If rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer timer expires and no PsUser_UserModifyReq (associated to PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd) is received, L2-PS assumes that the reconfiguration has been rejected by CP-RT and it restarts the channel monitoring which was stopped at PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd transmission.

If PsUser_UserModifyReq (associated to PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd) is received while rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer timer is running, rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer timer is stopped.

#### 2.1.4.15.0-5 User Reconfiguration Required User Reconfiguration required for sparse SSSG (ID: 12798424)

**2.1.4.15.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12798425`)

User Reconfiguration Required **[Before PR867429]**

L2-PS trigger PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd with sssgReconfigurationInd for sparseSssgSwitchingConfig update.

L2-PS start rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer to wait PsUser_UserModifyReq from CP-RT, common message flow refer to [11180113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5BPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)/[1144993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_238pvvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

1.If PsUser_UserModifyReq->l2psRequiredIndTrigger is sssgReconfiguration:

else

if CP-RT request to cancel the reconfiguration (PsUser_UserModifyReq->cancellationType is sssgReconfiguration),L2 PS stop current reconfiguration procedure, re-evaluation SSSG switching algorithm again.

2.If rdReconfigRequiredIndTimer is expires when waiting PsUser_UserModifyReq with sssgReconfiguration, L2 PS stop current reconfiguration procedure, re-enable SSSG switching evaluation algorithm again.

### 2.1.4.17 DRB Modify

#### 2.1.4.17.0-2 DRB Modify Critical bearer modification (ID: 13397864)

**2.1.4.17.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13397865`)

DRB Modify L2-PS shall check the criticality of the bearers requested for setup as mentioned below

1\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_DrbModifyReq-> drbModifyReqP[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as critical DRBs and SRBs.

2\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = True and DRBs part of PsUser_DrbModifyReq-> drbModifyReqP[] have their criticalDrbSchedEnabled = False, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

3\. If the cell configuration has actCriticalTraffic = False and DRBs part of PsUser_DrbModifyReq-> drbModifyReqP[] have their criticality flag criticalDrbSchedEnabled = True, L2-PS shall print a warning message, those respective DRBs and corresponding SRBs are marked as non critical DRBs and SRBs.

Note : SRB criticality is decide in three phases.

Phase1 : When there is no DRB. In this phase SRB criticality is decided by its flag criticalSrbSchedEnabled.

Phase2 : When a DRB is setup, SRB criticality is decided by the DRB such that if one or more DRBs are marked with criticalDrbSchedEnabled = true, then the mapping SRB is also considered critical irrespective of its criticalSrbSchedEnabled status.

Phase3: When the last DRB is removed, SRB is considered non critical

---

**2.1.4.19.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13285390`)

User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication Upon reception of a valid PsUser_BufferMonitoringInd message ([10978152](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VRj0Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 5G-L2-PS shall perform following actions:

  1. If the bufferMonitoring parameter is set to [Before CB012554-A] "activate-dl", "activate-ul", or "activate-dlAndul" [CB012554-A] caActivateDl, caActivateUl, caActivateDlAndUl, [End CB012554-A] the 5G-L2-PS shall act, as specified in requirement [11162664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25hXCfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  2. [CB012554-A] If bufferMonitoring parameters is set to tputBasedHoActivateDl, 5G-L2-PS shall act as specified in requirement [13284489: Starting DL buffer status monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2tcBAcuTEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB012554-A]
  3. If the bufferMonitoring parameter is set to [Before CB012554-A] "deactivate-dl" [CB012554-A] caDeactivateDl, [End CB012554-A] the 5G-L2-PS shall perform following actions:
  4. Stop DL buffer monitoring for SCell Configuration according to [11162704](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25h-EPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
  5. Remove the DL Pathloss reference from the UE context.
  6. [CB012554-A] If bufferMonitoring parameters is set to tputBasedHo-deactivate-dl, 5G-L2_PS shall stop DL buffer monitoring for inter-RAT handover purposes according to [13285486: Stopping DL bufer status monitoring](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_o3Ou0sxGEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB012554-A]

### 2.1.4.20 User Buffer Criterion Indication

#### 2.1.4.20.0-2 User Buffer Criterion Indication The buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition has been met (ID: 11146126)

**2.1.4.20.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13282866`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication When DL or UL buffer overflow condition is met and the data cannot be drained by the serving cell, 5G-L2-PS shall perform the following actions based on the specific data direction (DL or UL):

  1. 5G-L2-PS shall indicate to C-Plane that the buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition has been met for the corresponding direction.
  2. [CB014587-B]and conditionally include dlPathlossDiff according to [11162737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25h-FfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). [End CB014587-B]
  3. After sending the indication for a specific direction, 5G-L2-PS shall stop data buffer monitoring for that direction.



Data buffer monitoring for the other direction shall continue in parallel and unaffected.

Ref: [10978197: User Buffer Criterion Indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VRj2vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

#### 2.1.4.20.0-3 User Buffer Criterion Indication Buffer overflow criterion for Inter-RAT handover purposes (ID: 13284483)

**2.1.4.20.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13362282`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication When DL overflow condition is met and the data cannot be drained, 5G-L2-PS shall perform the following actions:

  1. 5G-L2-PS shall stop data buffer monitoring.
  2. 5G-L2-PS shall indicate to C-Plane that the buffer overflow criterion for inter-RAT handover has are met.

#### 2.1.4.20.0-4 User Buffer Criterion Indication Sending User Buffer Criterion Indication based on PCell radio link quality checks (ID: 11146136)

**2.1.4.20.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12811818`)

After this indication is sent, 5G-L2-PS [CB010741-A] DL [End CB010741] shall stop PCell radio link quality monitoring (see 5G_L2_13084_replaced([11162802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25ilIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

### 2.1.4.24 RAN measurements

#### 2.1.4.24.0-1 RAN measurements FA: [EFS] User Context Management Creator: Marta Nowosad (Nokia) Document Owner: TBD (ID: 13367253)

#### 2.1.4.24.1 Reception of PsUser_RanMeasurementReq

##### 2.1.4.24.1.0-1 Reception of PsUser_RanMeasurementReq RAN measurements reporting (ID: 13381932)

**2.1.4.24.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13381936`)

Reception of PsUser_RanMeasurementReq E-CID Ran measurements request provides per UE various UL on demand [CB014535-B] or periodic [End CB014535-B] measurement(s) from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT. Upon reception of the request PsUser_RanMeasurementReq:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall verify what kind of measurement was requested. Below measurement(s) may be requested:
  * timing advanced ([13367309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ziURcfbYEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ)) / [CB014535-A] accumulated timing advance ([13367743](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_cuEOZPdYEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ)) [End CB014535-A]
  * angle of arrival ([13367318](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_swos0fbZEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ))
  * SSB ([13367315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_mByPMvbZEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ))
  * 5G-L2-PS shall immediately send measurement(s) report in PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ([13367260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FMaY0_bSEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ)).



[CB014535-B]

For periodic only:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall start timer(s) ecidPeriodicitySsbAndAccTA ([13375113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wltVwPwPEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)) , ecidPeriodicityAoA ([13379122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_EL6eYf3TEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)), rdEcidAggregWindow ([13408130](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EOIHUQ5aEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). accordingly as in the activity diagram: [13438516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FrzPEiK6EfGbZ5_vsUrUNw)
  * 5G-L2-PS shall collect requested data with the most current data (refer to [13438516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CPI68yK6EfGbZ5_vsUrUNw) ) and add to PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd
  * 5G-L2-PS shall send measurement(s) report in PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd ([13367261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JPpkwvbSEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ)).



[End CB014535-B]

The ellipsis (...) suggests that these are parameterized periodicities. * **ecidPeriodicity(...)_X - rdEcidAggregWindow and ecidPeriodicity(...)_Y - rdtcidAggregWindow:** These labels, also in yellow and purple blocks respectively, represent specific time windows or processing periods associated with UE X and UE Y, possibly involving some form of aggregation or reduction. * **Agg Wind:** Short for "Aggregation Window," these smaller blocks indicate periods where data from UE X and UE Y might be aggregated. * **Bundled Ind UES X+Y:** This label suggests an indication or notification that bundles data or events from both UE X and UE Y. * **Red Brackets:** Red brackets are used to visually group or indicate the duration of certain periodicities or windows, specifically for UE X and UE Y. **Diagrammatic Representation:** The diagram uses horizontal bars to represent time intervals or ongoing processes. The flowchart begins with a request for UE measurements, followed by a response. A timer is started and then expires, leading to the initiation of an aggregation window. The process then checks if a bundled measurement report is being built. If the report is not being built, its content is constructed, and required data is collected and added. The aggregation window expires, and a check is performed to see if the bundled report was sent. If it was not sent, the UE sends the bundled report. If the report is being built, required data is collected and added to the ongoing report. A check is then made to see if the number of information elements (IEs) has been exceeded. If the limit is not exceeded, the UE sends the bundled report. If the limit is exceeded, the aggregation window expires. The flowchart also includes conditions for the expiry of periodicity settings (SsbAndAccTA or PeriodicityAoA). The text within the flowchart describes the steps and conditions of the process. ##### 2.1.4.24.1.0-6 Reception of PsUser_RanMeasurementReq UL Angle of Arrival measurement reporting (ID: 13367318)

**2.1.4.24.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13367320`)

Reception of PsUser_RanMeasurementReq [Before CB008577-E]Only [End Cb008577-E] FR1-TDD

UL Angle of Arrival measurement for UL NR E-CID is enabled when PsUser_RanMeasurementReq is received with:

  * for on demand angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE
  * [CB014535-B] for periodic angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE and ecidPeriodicityAoA ([13379122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_EL6eYf3TEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)) [End CB014535-B]



and cellTechnology=TDD in PsCell_CellSetupReq is received then 5G-L2-PS shall:

  * UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam(5G_UP_ALG_25322) for a requested UE
  * check whether there is valid DFT beam (bestH and bestV) during ulAoAMonitorWindow
  * if exist valid DFT beams, only the latest DFT beam corresponding
  * else if no valid DFT beams, dominant UL SSB/refine beam corresponding aoaH and aoaV ([Before CB008577-D]PsCell_CellSsbRefineBeamDoaInd [CB008577-D] PsCell_CellSsbRefinePmiBeamDoaInd [End CB008577-D]for SSB)
  * fill angleOfArrivalNrResult for the UE
  * send
  * for on demand PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ([10978473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
  * [CB014535-B] for periodic PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ([10978473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) for the first time and then periodic PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd ([13367261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JPpkwvbSEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ)).**[End CB014535-B]**



[CB008577-E]

FR1-FDD: for On-demand [CB014535-SR-B-UPD002] and periodic [CB014535-SR-B-UPD002]

When PsUser_RanMeasurementReq with:

  * for on demand angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE
  * [CB014535-SR-B-UPD002] for periodic angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE and ecidPeriodicityAoA ([13379122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_EL6eYf3TEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)) [End CB014535-SR-B-UPD002]



and cellTechnology=FDD with actBeamforming = TRUE in PsCell_CellSetupReq is received, then 5G-L2-PS shall report UL Angle of Arrival by filling angleOfArrivalNrResult for the UE in PsUser_RanMeasurementResp, the UL angle of Arrival value shall be as per [11156193: Maintain of dominant UL Beam for UE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2499YfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[End CB008577-E]

#### 2.1.4.24.2 Sending of PsUser_RanMeasurementResp

##### 2.1.4.24.2.0-2 Sending of PsUser_RanMeasurementResp 5G-L2-PS shall send measurement(s) report for the UE depend on E-CID report characteristics: for on demand PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ( 10978473 ) [CB014535-B] for periodic PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ( 10978473 ) for the first time and then periodic PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd ( 13367261 ).[End CB014535-B] with required report(s) according to PsUser_RanMeasurementReq ( 13367259 ): ssbBeamIdResult tAdvMeasResult angleOfArrivalNrResult When  PsUser_RanMeasurementReq with: angleOfArrivalNrRequired=FALSE is received, then 5G-L2-PS shall omit angleOfArrivalNrResult in PsUser_RanMeasurementResp [Before CB014535-A] tAdvMeasRequired = FALSE [CB014535-A] tAdvMeasRequired = disabled [End CB014535-A] is received, then 5G-L2-PS shall omit tAdvMeasResult in PsUser_RanMeasurementResp ssbBeamIdRequired=FALSE is received, then 5G-L2-PS shall omit ssbBeamIdResult in PsUser_RanMeasurementResp. Expected exceptions see: 10978444 . (ID: 13367282)

##### 2.1.4.24.3.0-2 Indication of PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd List of UEs measurement results in PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd (ID: 13473158)

**2.1.4.24.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13473159`)

Indication of PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd 5G-L2-PS shall send PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd with list of UEs measurement results (IE ueMeasurement ([13339164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_2Ps3FNs0EfCmxLW1M7HMrQ)) ) in one bundle message. Requested measurement(s) per UE in PsUser_RanMeasurementReq may be send in the same or different list of UEs measurement results in one bundle message PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd or different bundle messages PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd because different collection time in aggregation window rdEcidAggregWindow ([13408130](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EOIHUQ5aEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and sequential order of 5G-L2-PS command execution. Refer to 13438516 with activity with periodic timers dependency.

5G-L2-PS shall send periodic measurement(s) report in PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd on SICAD address received in IE ranMeasAddress in PsCnfg_AddressDistributionReq ([10966093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UL-vvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

If number of IE ueMeasurement is exceeded in PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd,

then 5G-L2-PS shall send PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd during rdEcidAggregWindow

else

refer to [13438516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CPI68yK6EfGbZ5_vsUrUNw) with activity with periodic timers dependency.

##### 2.1.4.24.3.0-3 Indication of PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd Stop reporting PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd (ID: 13473160)

**2.1.4.24.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13473161`)

Indication of PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd If 5G-L2-PS receive any other PsUser_RanMeasurementReq ([10978459)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) for the same UE with:

  * ssbBeamIdRequired = FALSE
  * angleOfArrivalNrRequired = FALSE
  * tAdvMeasRequired = disabled



then 5G-L2-PS shall stop timer(s) ecidPeriodicitySsbAndAccTA ([13375113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wltVwPwPEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)) , ecidPeriodicityAoA ([13379122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_EL6eYf3TEfCPDo8cGBoqIw)), rdEcidAggregWindow ([13408130](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EOIHUQ5aEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and stop sending periodic measurement(s) report for this UE from PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd.

When 5G-L2-PS receives PsUser_UserDeleteReq [CB014535-B-UPD002] or for PsUser_UserDeleteReq during Intra-cell HO handover with a new Contention-Based / Contention-Free Random Access happend

[End CB014535-B-UPD002], then 5G-L2-PS shall:

  * stop all timers: ecidPeriodicitySsbAndAccTA , ecidPeriodicityAoA , rdEcidAggregWindow for the given UE
  * stop sending PsUser_RanBundledMeasReportInd for the given UE

  * 5G-L2-PS shall start periodic timer for the UE with timer duration set to (ecidPeriodicityAoA - rdEcidAggregWindow ([13408130](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EOIHUQ5aEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))) (accordingly as in the activity diagram: [13438516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FrzPEiK6EfGbZ5_vsUrUNw)) when PsUser_RanMeasurementReq ([10978459)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is received with angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE



At the next cycle:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall start periodic timer for the UE with timer duration set to ecidPeriodicityAoA (accordingly as in the activity diagram: [13438516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FrzPEiK6EfGbZ5_vsUrUNw)) when PsUser_RanMeasurementReq ([10978459)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is received with angleOfArrivalNrRequired=TRUE

---

**2.1.4.24.4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13379125`)
