## 2.1.6 Test Procedures

### 2.1.6.0-2 Test Procedures DL DCI Transmission Request to 5GUE-L2-SM (ID: 11146263)

**2.1.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146275`)

Test Procedures [Before CNI-109596]

When testing with Airphone, for each message DlData_PdcchSendReq towards 5G-L1-DL, 5G-L2-PS shall send, with the same timing, an exact copy to 5GUE-L2-SM (MSC 5G_L1L2_AP_67: DL HARQ Rx).Note that this message is called SmDataUe_PdcchInd on 5GUE-L2-SM, see 5G_L1L2_AP_287 the message DlData_PdcchSendReq is forwarded to 5GUE-L2-SM. See 5G_L1_5G21A_70 for description of DlData_PdcchSendReq message.

5G-L2-PS shall send DlData_PdcchSendReq towards 5GUE-L2-SM (i.e. SmDataUe_PdcchInd) only when smDataUePdcchIndAddress is available, i.e. PsTest_SubCellGroupInfoReq (see 5G_L2_IF_587_replaced([10978668](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VVOPfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) was received with a valid EQID address in the field smDataUePdcchIndAddress.

Note: 5G-L2-PS shall not expect to receive PsTest_SubCellGroupInfoReq from test UEs other than Airphone.

Note: 5GUE-L2-SM is L2 Scheduler Manager in the Airphone

See 5G_L1L2_AP_287 for a full description of the message SmDataUe_PdcchInd, including timing, addressing and preconditions

[End CNI-109596]

[CNI-109596]

The message SmDataUe_PdcchInd is no more used and has been removed.

[End CNI-109596]

### 2.1.10.1 PS Peer Control For inter-L2RT UL CA

#### 2.1.10.1.1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlSchedulingInd

##### 2.1.10.1.1.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlSchedulingInd SCell get UE's PCell UL/DL scheduling result (ID: 11146364)

**2.1.10.1.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12621155`)

PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlSchedulingInd For a UL CA UE, when SCell schedules a UL slot, the SCell set the prediction that no PUSCH scheduled for the UE in PCell on the overlapping slot by default. The SCell should multiplexing all the UE’s DL HARQ bit and periodic CSI report bit on the UL slot. Under default precondition, the number of multiplexed DL HARQ bit is estimated according DPA’s maximum tDai as 5G_L2_598_replaced([11158391](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KxvPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) across all the UE’s serving cell.

For UL scheduling a newTx or reTx in PCell, SCell should restore the real PUSCH scheduling result for the UE in PCell for this overlapping slot indicated by puschScheduled in the message as 5G_L2_IF_2130_replaced([10980097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmTvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If puschScheduled = DedicatedGrant, then both DL HARQ bit and possible CSI bit should be multiplexed on PCell’s PUSCH, and _numOfHarqDBitsForPusch as 5G_L2_IF_2130_replaced([10980097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmTvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is not used by SCell._

For UE with DL scheduling but no UL scheduling in PCell on the HARQ feedback overlapping UL slot, SCell should restore the default DL HARQ bit number with _numOfHarqDBitsForPusch for L1 receive request if puschScheduled = None on this overlapping slot as 5G_L2_IF_2130_replaced([10980097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VfmTvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

If UE is scheduled PUSCH in PCell by Configured Grant in overlapping UL slot _(PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlSchedulingInd.puschScheduled = ConfiguredGrant), SCell shall handle multiplexing of DL HARQ bits (if any,_ PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlSchedulingInd._numOfHarqDBitsForPusch) and periodic CSI bits (if any, based on_ PsPeerCtrl_PcellCsiStatusInd.perCsiSyncInfo) **in PuschReceiveReq message for L1.** ****

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a table with a blue header row and blue column headers. The table has three columns: "PUSCH", "UCI (A/N bits, CSI)", and "PCell", "SCell". The "PUSCH" column is further divided into "PCell" and "SCell". The table has six rows of data. Here is the data in the table:

PUSCH (PCell) | PUSCH (SCell) | UCI (A/N bits, CSI)  
---|---|---  
None | None | Pcell PUCCH  
None | Dedicated Grant | Scell PUSCH  
Dedicated Grant | None | Pcell PUSCH  
Dedicated Grant | Dedicated Grant | Pcell PUSCH  
Configured Grant | None | Pcell PUSCH  
Configured Grant | Dedicated Grant | Scell PUSCH  
  
Notes: [Before PR831845]it's not applied to FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA refer to 5G_L2_7108_replaced([11160809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25W-_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[PR831845]

  1. It's not applied to FR1 TDD + FDD UL CA refer to 5G_L2_7108_replaced([11160809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25W-_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  2. For FR1 TDD + FR1 TDD UL CA with tdLteConfig0 frame structure, due to the value of DL and UL scheduling slotOffset increased(refer to [11157417: tdLte Config0 frame structure timing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25FSLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), more buffered slots of PcellUlSchedulingInd info are required before SCell DL send out PuschReceiveReq to L1.




[End PR831845]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.2 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlBufferSplitInd

##### 2.1.10.1.2.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlBufferSplitInd SCell update Ue's buffer (ID: 11146405)

**2.1.10.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146418`)

PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlBufferSplitInd For a UL CA UE, the Ul data source can be only from buffer split by PCell via PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlBufferSplitInd 5G_L2_IF_2140_replaced([10980170](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VgNXfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Once receiving the buffer split from PCell, SCell should:

1\. Validate the message sequence by validating bufferSplitProcessSN: bufferSplitProcessSN from message should = bufferSplitProcessSN in local context + 1. After the validation, store bufferSplitProcessSN from message as bufferSplitProcessSN in local context.

[Before PR666385]

2\. Store rrmBufferSplitBaseTime： store UE’s sfnReport and slotReport from message as rrmBufferSplitBaseTime.xsfn; store a corresponding rrmBufferSplitBaseTime.Tsc;

[PR666385]

2\. Store rrmLastUlBsrUpdateTime: store UE's hfnReport, sfnReport and slotReport from message as rrmLastUlBsrUpdateTime.xhfn; store a corresponding rrmLastUlBsrUpdateTime.Tsc;

[End PR666385]

3\. Update its overall buffer and buffer for its LCGs:

rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_byte = rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes;

rrmScheduledUlData_bytes = 0;

rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes[i] = bufferInByte[i]; with i as the LCG index.

[Before PR666385]

4\. With update rrmBufferSplitBaseTime, do housekeeping statistics:

[PR666385]

4\. With update rrmLastUlBsrUpdateTime, do housekeeping statistics:

[End PR666385]

Checking the not released HARQ in harq pool. If the initial transmission time for the HARQ is later than rrmBufferSplitBaseTime as calculation of 5G_L2_7630_replaced([11161327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then the scheduled bytes in this HARQ is belong to this buffer split process:

rrmScheduledUlData_bytes += tbSize in the HARQ;

5\. [CB006137-BA] If initialSplitTxPower present, update initial power and adjustment step in mw, triggered by case1/2/3. 5G_UP_ALG_10879_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [END CB006137-BA]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.3 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd

##### 2.1.10.1.3.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd SCell restore UE's PHR (ID: 11146429)

**2.1.10.1.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146442`)

PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd When UL CA UE’s PHR is reported on PCell, SCell receives it from PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd as 5G_L2_IF_2675_replaced([10980241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vg0bPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UE in SCell use hfnReport, sfnReport, slotReport in the message to check whether this PHR is the most recent one compared with local latest PHR report time. If it is the most recent PHR, then store the PHR most recent time as hfnReport, sfnReport, slotReport and use the powerHeadRoomLevel, pcmax for UE’s SCell UL LA.

When using powerHeadRoomLevel, pcmax, the parameter like numOfPRB for corresponding PHR should be sync on the same initial transmission on slot hfnReport, sfnReport, slotReport. If there are multiple overlapping UL slots in SCell corresponding to one slot hfnReport, sfnReport, slotReport in PCell, SCell shall handle the PHR using the initial transmission PRB information of the first PUSCH slot, refer to 3GPP 38.213 7.7.1.

[Before CB006137-BC]

Due to no closed loop power control, PHR information forwarded from PCell is not used to calc UL pathloss in SCell.

[CB006137-BC]

The PHR information forwarded from PCell will be used to calculate DL pathloss for UL RLQ resume and UL pathloss for closed loop power control in SCell.

[End CB006137-BC]

[CB006137-BA] If efficiencyRequest present, Indicating a list of UE that the efficiencyPerPRB on Scell are needed, UEs in this efficiencyRequest need to calculate the efficiencyPerPRB on Scell and sent the efficiencyPerPRB to pcell with psPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd [END CB006137-BA]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.4 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd

##### 2.1.10.1.4.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd PCell update after UE's SCell Ul Scheduling (ID: 11146456)

**2.1.10.1.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146469`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd For inter-L2RT UL CA UE, the overall buffer is controlled by PCell, PCell get the SCell real time buffer information by PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlHousekeepingReportInd as 5G_L2_IF_2366_replaced([10980622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vj3t_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Store SCell’s eTH in PCell with the present eTh from UE’s SCell in the message.

Validate the housekeeping report sequence and store SCell’s buffer information:

if bufferSplitProcessSN from SCell in the message < bufferSplitProcessSN in PCell:

the buffer information in this message for SCell is dropped by PCell;

else if bufferSplitProcessSN from SCell in the message = bufferSplitProcessSN in PCell:

store the UE’s SCell buffer information in PCell as bellow:

rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_byte for SCell = rrmBufferedDataUlTotalBytes in the message;

rrmScheduledUlData_bytes for SCell = rrmScheduledUlDataBytes in the message ;

rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes[i] = rrmBufferedDataUlLcgBytes[i] in the message; with i as the LCG index;

record the SCell buffer information update time as sfn, slotPusch in the message.

Calculate that if trigger-3 in 5G_UP_ALG_10281_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) can be triggered after the buffer information is updated.

[CB006137-BA] If scellIncreasingPower present , set scell requireMorePower = true for over power check purpose, decrease the pcell splitTxPower with scellIncreasingPower if scellIncreasingPower > 0 [END CB006137-BA]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.5 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlSchedulingInd

##### 2.1.10.1.5.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlSchedulingInd SCell send UL scheduling result to PCell (ID: 11146483)

**2.1.10.1.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146489`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlSchedulingInd When SCell UL FD scheduler complete the UL grant handling on an overlapping UL slot, it shall construct the message PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlSchedulingInd refer to 5G_L2_IF_2149_replaced([10980319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vhbefu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), which including all of UL CA UE’s RNTI that are granted (both newTx and reTx are included) on an overlapping UL slot. PCell decide if PUCCH is needed for UL CA UE based on this message, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9538_replaced([11204208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3609_replaced([11159986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For PCell DL, if UL CA UE is included in the sCellSchedulingInfo in PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlSchedulingInd, PCell shall no longer handle the UCI information of this UE on the overlapping UL slot since it's already mutiplexed on SCell PUSCH, otherwise PCell shall handle the UL CA UE's UCI information over PCell's PUCCH.

---

#### 2.1.10.1.6 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD

##### 2.1.10.1.6.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD SCell forward UL CA UEs HarqD info to Pcell (ID: 11146501)

**2.1.10.1.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146509`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD On overlapping UL slot, If HARQ Ack/Nack bits over SCell PUSCH, SCell DL will receive UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD of scheduled UL CA UEs. SCell shall forward UL CA UEs’ HarqD info to PCell via PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD as per 5G_L2_IF_2167_replaced([10980475](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VipmPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: There are two possible messages on one UL slot because 5G-L1 does not bundle Format1 and Format3 in same message UlData_PuschReceivedRespHarqD.

---

##### 2.1.10.1.6.0-2 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD Pcell handle UL CA UEs HarqD info forwarded from SCell (ID: 11146515)

**2.1.10.1.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146529`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschHarqD When receive this forward message, PCell shall:

 extract the HARQ Ack/Nack bits,

 handle the HARQ Ack/Nack bits belonging to PCell itself,

 forward the SCell’s HARQ Ack/Nack bits to specific SCell via PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuXchReceiveIndHarqD, refer to 5G_L2_IF_667_replaced([10979675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vci__u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 [CB009189-B] perform counter handling as described in 5G_L2_8084_replaced([11150707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8086_replaced([11150721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8099_replaced([11150731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_8101_replaced([11150745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009189-B].

---

#### 2.1.10.1.7 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs

##### 2.1.10.1.7.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs SCell forward UL CA UEs pCSI info to Pcell (ID: 11146541)

**2.1.10.1.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146549`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs On overlapping UL slot, if period CSI report (Channel acquisition or Beam report) over SCell PUSCH, SCell UL will receive UlData_PuschReceivedRespPs of scheduled UL CA UEs. SCell shall forward UL CA UEs’ period CSI report info to PCell via PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs as per 5G_L2_IF_2176_replaced([10980518](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VjQofu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For the UL measurement information from UlData_PuschReceivedRespPs, SCell UL shall forward them to SCell DL via puschReceiveRespPsLight as per 5G_L2_5746_replaced([11242493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BrNePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.1.10.1.7.0-2 PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs PCell handle pCSI info forwarded from SCell (ID: 11146558)

**2.1.10.1.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146563`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellForwardPuschPs When receive this forward message, PCell shall handle the period CSI report bits belonging to PCell itself and forward the SCell’s period CSI report bits to specific SCell via PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuschReceiveIndPs, refer to 5G_L2_IF_672_replaced([10979726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VdKCfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.1.10.1.8 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd

##### 2.1.10.1.8.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd SCell Update UL CA UEs Info to Pcell (ID: 11146575)

**2.1.10.1.8.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11146609`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd when SCell receive LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd (refer to 5G_L2_IF_875_replaced([10984687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBxzvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SCell shall send this message PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd(refer to 5G_L2_IF_2158_replaced([10980365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2ViCg_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to PCell if any of the following conditions is fulfilled:

(1) If SCell receive UL BSR MAC CE of UL CA UE, SCell shall forward all LCG specific buffer size to PCell to evaluate UE’s buffer status for UL buffer split, as per 5G_UP_ALG_10514_replaced([11203665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(2) If SCell receive PHR MAC CE of UL CA UE, SCell shall handle SCell’s PHR itself, and forward PCell's PHR to PCell. PCell shall compare the hyperSfn/sfn/slot from ueUpdateInfo with last updated PHR's initial time(rrmLastPhrUpdateXhfn) to ensure only the latest PHR is handled. Then find the initial transmission PRB information based on the initial time and handle the PHR as legacy procedure.

[CB012149-CA]For FR1 R15 UL CA UE with TDD PCell and FDD SCell, SCell doesn't forward PCell's PHR. Rationale: UE will not be scheduled parallelly on Pcell and Scell in Ul overlapping slots, therefore SCell never receives PCell's real PHR; and PCell does not use virtual PHR.

After the FR1 UL CA allow-list introduced(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_25188_replaced([11208767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwwQQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), parallel scheduling is possible. Therefore, for FR1 R15 UL CA UE with TDD PCell and FDD SCell, SCell shall forward PCell's non virtual PHR to PCell.[End CB012149-CA]

(3) If SCell identifies LCG over transmission as per 5G_UP_ALG_9787_replaced([11203724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), based on the amount of data received per logical channel in an UL transport block from LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd, SCell shall send the over transmission bytes per LCG to PCell. PCell shall subtract overReceivedBytes[k] from rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes[k] in PCell, k is the logic group ID. For more details refer to 5G_L2_7632_replaced([11161348](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25apV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(4) If SCell identifies NACK Flood Denfense as 5G_UP_ALG_4892_replaced([11197752](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwH-JvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), or exit NACK Flood Defense as 5G_L2_8747_replaced([11163820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25or0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), SCell shall inform PCell about the NACK Flood Defense event.

If SCell is deactivated, no need to sync NACK Flood Exit event to Pcell anymore(If SCell deactivation happens after entering NFD state).

PCell shall store SCell’s NFD state as UE SCell specific flag -- isScellInNfdState.

By default PCell store isScellInNfdState as false.

When receiving SCell's NFD event, PCell shall update SCell’s isScellInNfdState according to NFD event. If event is ENTERNFD, set isScellInNfdState as true, otherwise, set isScellInNfdState as false.

PCell should do NFD data re-split trigger check as 5G_UP_ALG_14522_replaced([11122787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if the UE's state is one CC NFD after the event handling.

(5) If SCell receives a Mac CE for CG activation or CG deactivation, SCell shall inform PCell about the reception of this Mac CE.

On reception of PeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd with IE isConfiguredGrantConfCe present, PCell triggers MacCEForActivationDeactivation event in CG state machine (ref 5G_L2_10641_replaced([11176201](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26x7TPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_9693_replaced([11176176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26x7R_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_9685_replaced([11176139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26xUP_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB005935-BD]

(6) If SCell receives PsUser_RrcReconfCompletedReq with transformPrecoderSwitchInd set to "success" meaning Transform Precoder state has changed (see 5G_L2_IF_2575_replaced([10977732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VOghfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SCell shall inform PCell whether the Transform Precoder is active on SCell.

On reception of PeerCtrl_ScellUlInfoUpdateInd with IE isUlScellTransformPrecoderAct present, PCell stores that information in UE context and evaluates UL CA buffer split (5G_UP_ALG_22286_replaced([11173280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuSLGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and/or deactivates Configured Grant (5G_UP_ALG_24791_replaced([11173371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuSyI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB005935-BD]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.9 PsPeerCtrl_PcellTaSync

##### 2.1.10.1.9.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellTaSync PCell query/reset timing advance result from/in Scell (ID: 11146624)

**2.1.10.1.9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13487568`)

PsPeerCtrl_PcellTaSync When Scell receive message, For UEs from _ueTaSyncInfo in PsPeerCtrl_PcellTaSync:_

If action == taQuery, then

Scell response _puschLongTermTimingOffset/puschWeight [CB015279-F] and/or srsLongTermTimingOffset/srsWeight [End CB015279-F]to Pcell via psPeerCtrl_ScellTaReport. Then Pcell computes TAC based on [Before CB015279-F] both LTO both from Scell and Pcell [CB015279-F] LTO from PCell and/or LTO from response (dependent on TAG SCell belongs to) [End CB015279-F], refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3316_replaced([11150211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksSnB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB015279-F] and [13442072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FzQo4CWiEfGxldjOZQLezQ) [End CB015279-F]._

or else if action == taReset, 

Scell reset timing advance result of itself.

---

#### 2.1.10.1.10 PsPeerCtrl_ScellTaReport

##### 2.1.10.1.10.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellTaReport Scell report timing advance result to PCell (ID: 11146644)

**2.1.10.1.10.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13487587`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellTaReport Scell report its timing advance result to PCell. this procedure is triggered by PsPeerCtrl_PcellTaSync when action == taQuery.

Timing advance result include [Before CB015279-F] the [End CB015279-F] PUSCH long term timing offset [Before CB015279-F] and the [CB015279-F] , [End CB015279-F] PUSCH weight [CB015279-F] , SRS long term timing offset and SRS wieght [End CB015279-F] on SCell.

If PUSCH long term timing offset is invalid (no valid PUSCH timing offset measurement on SCell), SCell shall response a invalid value(float nan) in _puschLongTermTimingOffset in this message [CB015279-F] , If SRS long term timing offset is invalid (no valid SRS timing offset measurement on SCell), SCell shall respond with invalid value(float nan) in_ srsLongTermTimingOffset in this message (Note: SRS long term timing offset can be valid only on SCell configured with sTAG , see: [13442072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FzQo4CWiEfGxldjOZQLezQ)) [End CB015279-F]. For details refer to 5G_L1L2_FLOW_1296_replaced([11201582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BgSozvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

---

#### 2.1.10.1.11 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd

##### 2.1.10.1.11.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd scell update Ue's UL power control info (ID: 11146666)

**2.1.10.1.11.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146674`)

PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd For a UL CA UE, the ul power control info from PCell via psPeerCtrl_PcellUlPowerCtrlInd(5G_L2_IF_2905_replaced([10980880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vls7_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received in SCell, then it should be handled as:

  1. if pcellIncreasingPower present, scell splitTxPower should be decreased by pcellIncreasingPower if pcell powerState not suspend, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10881_replaced([11119868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  2. if newPcellSplitPowerAdjStep/newScellSplitPowerAdjStep present, new pcell/scell splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep applied in scell for the purpose of split TX power adjustment(5G_UP_ALG_10881_replaced([11119868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and calculation of the suspend condition1 by using pcell/scell splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep instead of pcell/scell efficiencyPerPRB in 5G_UP_ALG_10921_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




[CB006137-BC]

  1. If the minPrbSplitTxPower is present, it's calculated based on nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB and minNumPrbsUl (and the maximum TPC value if PUSCH CLPC enabled) in PCell.



\- SCell will firstly calculate the splitTxPower from the received minPrbSplitTxPower as described in 5G_UP_ALG_10923_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and then calculate the prbBasedOnSpecifiedSplitPower from the splitTxPower as described in 5G_UP_ALG_10883_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- SCell will use the prbBasedOnSpecifiedSplitPower in Pcell resume check during evaluation period(rdPeriodForOverPowerEva), refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10923_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  1. If pcellSuspend is present, it means PCell Ul scheduling suspend due to condition2, SCell could use full split tx power in next overlapping slot and start the PCell resume check procedure, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10921_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



[End CB006137-BC]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.12 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlControlInd

##### 2.1.10.1.12.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlControlInd pcell update Ue's UL control info (ID: 11146688)

**2.1.10.1.12.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146693`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUlControlInd For a UL CA UE, the ul control info from SCell via psPeerCtrl_ScellUlControlInd(5G_L2_IF_2944_replaced([10980976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vm7A_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received in PCell, then it should be handled as:

  1. if (powerState == Normal)



omit the field of powerState and the initialSplitTxPower in this msg.

else if (powerState == Suspend)

set pcell powerState = suspend

else if (powerState == Resume)

set pcell powerState = Resume

set the pcell splitTxPower = initialSplitTxPower, which triggered by case4 in 5G_UP_ALG_10879_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB006137-BB]

  1. If rlqStatus present, store the SCell Ul rlqStatus in PCell.



When rlqStatus is bad, PCell Ul will trigger Ul buffer split stop and suspend SCell Ul scheduling by sending PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlBufferSplitInd.

When rlqStatus is good, PCell Ul will trigger Ul buffer split and resume SCell Ul scheduling.

[End CB006137-BB]

---

#### 2.1.10.1.13 PsPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd

##### 2.1.10.1.13.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd PCell receive ScellEffciencyReportInd with efficiencyPerPrb (ID: 11146707)

**2.1.10.1.13.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146715`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd For a UL CA UE, efficiencyPerPrb from SCell via psPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd(5G_L2_IF2926) received in PCell, it should be handled for the purpose of Split TX power adjustment step calculation, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_10877_replaced([11119861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

psPeerCtrl_ScellEfficiencyReportInd be sent in response to PsPeerCtrl_PcellUlPhrForwardInd with efficiencyRequest present(5G_L2_IF_2675_replaced([10980241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vg0bPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) received in SCell.

### 2.1.10.2 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation

#### 2.1.10.2.0-1 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Maximum message size (ID: 11146728)

**2.1.10.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146735`)

Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation The maximum size of PsPeerCtrl messages used for IgNB CA (see 5G_L2_IF_2688_replaced([10980851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vls6vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not exceed 1168 bytes (due to transport constraints from NR IgNB CA payload over Xp unreliable messages/UDP) – see 5G_UP_ALG_2934_replaced([11123848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql97_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and Xp protocol specification at <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/Xpapplicationprotocol/Shared%20Documents/Xp%20application%20protocol%20specification.>

Each PsPeerCtrl message listed as an IE (member) of extendible union in 5G_L2_IF_2688_replaced([10980851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vls6vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be split if maximum message size with required extra space for extension points (see 5G_L2_IF_2788_replaced([10979146](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VY4mPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) would exceed the aforementioned limit. 

To keep a message size below its limit:

 The nested IE lists within the message shall have reduced maximum length (number of elements) and extra space shall be reserved for the extension points according to the 5G_L2_IF_2788_replaced([10979146](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VY4mPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The messages shall be split, if necessary, so one message carries less amount of information (e.g. just for one slot instead of multiple, see 5G_UP_ALG_2934_replaced([11123848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kql97_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), or for less number of UEs).

 5G-L2-PS can send the reduced size messages in subsequent slots, if it is possible according to the DPA timers (see 5G_L2_593_replaced([11158186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKpvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_595_replaced([11158240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25KKrvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 2.1.10.2.0-2 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Transmission of PsPeerCtrl_ScellDrbStopReq (ID: 11146742)

**2.1.10.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146751`)

Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation If 5G_L2-PS is triggered by 5G_L2_8581_replaced([11146074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXaPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to send PsPeerCtrl_ScellDrbStopReq message (5G_L2_IF_3379_replaced([10981099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VniHfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it shall set:

 pCellNrCellIdentity to the nrCellIdentity,

 sCellNrCellIdentity to the ext-SCell’s cell ID corresponding to servingCellIndex,

 ueIdDu to the same,

 rnti to the UE’s RNTI corresponding to crnti,

 logicalChannelIdentity to the same,

as received in the triggering message.

---

#### 2.1.10.2.0-3 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellDrbStopReq (ID: 11146758)

**2.1.10.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11146764`)

Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Upon reception of a valid PsPeerCtrl_ScellDrbStopReq message (5G_L2_IF_3379_replaced([10981099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VniHfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the 5G-L2-PS shall:

 send LoCtrl_StopFlowControlReq message (5G_L2_IF_895_replaced([10984902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WDm9_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8587_replaced([11181200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27SRkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to the 5G-L2-LO instance, which corresponds to the relevant SCell,

 follow 5G_UP_ALG_11592_replaced([11174551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kudKMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_9885_replaced([11175183](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuhbofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_4504_replaced([11179776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7ESfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G_UP_ALG_10158_replaced([11181155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku85ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with regards to DRB data scheduling.

---

#### 2.1.10.2.0-4 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep (ID: 11146770)

**2.1.10.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11146777`)

Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep message (see 5G_L2_IF_2118_replaced([10979995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ve_Pfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with syncStatus IE, the PCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall check ext-SCell’s synchronization status and proceed with further steps only if synchronization status has changed:

 follow ext-SCell deactivation procedure (see 5G_L2_16188_replaced([11163147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25kaYPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if received syncStatus is OutOfSync,

 follow ext-SCell reactivation procedure (see 5G_L2_16190_replaced([11163159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25kaYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if received syncStatus is InSync.

---

#### 2.1.10.2.0-5 Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq (ID: 11146786)

**2.1.10.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11146792`)

Inter-gNB Carrier Aggregation Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equal to deactivateExtScellOutOfSync on ext-SCell, the ext-SCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall:

 handle ext-SCell deactivation for each UE specified in request (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_316_replaced([11195925](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrZ_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 response via PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to PCell with list of successfully deactivated UEs.

When ext-Scell’s 5G-L2-PS receives PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message with modifType IE equal to start for ext-SCell reactivation due to synchronization status change to InSync (see 5G_L2_16190_replaced([11163159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25kaYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the ext-SCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall:

 handle ext-SCell reactivation for each UE specified in request (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_304_replaced([11195795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxEWfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 response via PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message to PCell with list of successfully reactivated UEs.

### 2.1.10.3 PS Peer Control for inter-L2RT DL CA

#### 2.1.10.3.1 PsPeerCtrl_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd

##### 2.1.10.3.1.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd SCell indication of UEs buffer statuses (ID: 11146815)

**2.1.10.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146820`)

PsPeerCtrl_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd When SCell receive LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd (5G_L2_IF_870_replaced([10984615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WBxwPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) it shall store received buffer status in local data storage.

SCell shall periodically, every rdPeriodDlUserBufferMessage TTI (5G_L2_7793_replaced([11181691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27V78_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), send PsPeerCtrl_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd message to the PCell with DL UE buffer statuses previously stored in local data storage.

SCell shall keep track of update sent to PCell to avoid sending not changed buffer statuses.

While filling PsPeerCtrl_DlScellUeBufferStatusInd message SCell shall prioritize UEs by last time the update for given UE was sent to the PCell (UE’s for which received buffer status report from SCell 5G-L2-LO was not sent for the longest time shall have higher priority).

---

#### 2.1.10.3.2 PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuXchReceiveIndHarqD

##### 2.1.10.3.2.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellPuXchReceiveIndHarqD HARQ feedback handling (ID: 11146834)

**2.1.10.3.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146847`)

 extract and handle the HARQ feedback as described in 5G_UP_ALG_4532_replaced([11184193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

  * [CB009189-B] update counters as described in 5G_L2_8084_replaced([11150707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8086_replaced([11150721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8099_replaced([11150731](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_8101_replaced([11150745](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24eOJvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB009189-B]

#### 2.1.10.3.3 PsPeerCtrl_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs

##### 2.1.10.3.3.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs CSI report forwarding (ID: 11146861)

**2.1.10.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146867`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs When P(S)cell forwards relevant CSI reports to an SCell (see 5G_L2_IF_678_replaced([10979801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VdxF_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) it shall send per single PsPeerCtrl_ScellPucchReceiveIndPs message the feedback for number of UEs equal to min(rdMaxNumUesPerSingleMsg, maxNumUeSingleMsg), see 5G_L2_8347_replaced([11181701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27V79fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_IF_680_replaced([10979816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VdxGvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of rdMaxNumUesPerSingleMsg less than maxNumUeSingleMsg shall be used only for testing purposes.

#### 2.1.10.3.4 PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep

##### 2.1.10.3.4.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep Measurement report forwarding (ID: 11146881)

**2.1.10.3.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146888`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep When Scell reports measurement result to Pcell (see 5G_L2_IF_2117_replaced([10979981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ve_Ovu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) it shall send per single PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep message the feedback for number of UEs equal to min(rdMaxNumUesPerSingleMsg, maxNumOfSCellAlloc), see 5G_L2_8347_replaced([11181701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27V79fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_IF_2118_replaced([10979995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ve_Pfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of rdMaxNumUesPerSingleMsg less than maxNumOfSCellAlloc shall be used only for testing purposes.

---

##### 2.1.10.3.4.0-2 PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep SCell load update and forwarding (ID: 11146897)

**2.1.10.3.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146902`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellMeasurementRep When PCell DL recieves Scell overload control countermeasure trigger result (see 5G_L2_IF_2117_replaced([10979981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ve_Ovu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell DL should update SCell's countermeasure triggers with latest sCellDlRtForbidActTrigger/sCellDlCoreOverloadTrigger/sCellUlRtForbidActTrigger/sCellUlCoreOverloadTrigger, and share the latest sCellUlRtStopDataTrigger to PCell UL.

---

### 2.1.10.4 SCell DL Non-Gbr UE Buffer Size Ind

#### 2.1.10.4.1 PsPeerCtrl_DlScellNonGbrUeBufferSizeInd

##### 2.1.10.4.1.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_DlScellNonGbrUeBufferSizeInd When 5G-L2-PS on SCell receives LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd ( 10984606 ), it shall store the received non-GBR DRBs estimated buffer size. 5G-L2-PS on SCell shall periodically, every rdPeriodDlUserBufferMessage ( 11181691 ) send PsPeerCtrl_DlScellNonGbrUeBufferSizeInd message to the 5G-L2-PS on PCell with DL non-GBR DRBs estimated buffer size. 5G-L2-PS on SCell shall keep track of update sent to 5G-L2-PS on PCell to avoid sending not changed buffer statuses. (ID: 13457355)

### 2.1.10.5 Intra-gNB Carrier Aggregation

#### 2.1.10.5.1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq

##### 2.1.10.5.1.0-1 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Transmission of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq (ID: 11146924)

**2.1.10.5.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146939`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Beam data synchronization triggered by SCell activation:

When SCell activation procedure is successfully completed (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_291_replaced([11195612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bfv2PvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_L2_623_replaced([11158897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25NOAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS instance checks below conditions:

 SCell is present in srsBfSyncStatusForScells, and,

 UE uses large BWP (see 5G_UP_ALG_1826_replaced([11110973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on PCell,

If all conditions are met, then 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 create or update (when second SCell is adding) rrmEligibleScellsList in UE context (see 5G_UP_ALG_17257_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_16753_replaced([11154964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 If SRS CoMa measured on Pcell is not aged (see 5G_L2_17305_replaced([11155038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242orfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then:

o if dedicated UE PCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) not started already, then start UE PCell timer,

o send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to related SCell according to section below: “Filling PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message”.

Beam data synchronization triggered by SRS Beam Manager:

When PCell’s DL scheduler receives PsInternal_SrsBeamSelectionInd message (see 5G_L2_6518_replaced([11243657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Bx7KPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from SRS beam manager, then 5G-L2-PS instance checks below conditions:

 SCell is present in rrmEligibleScellsList (see 5G_L2_16753_replaced([11154964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and,

 SRS CoMa measured on Pcell is not aged (see 5G_L2_17305_replaced([11155038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242orfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and,

 PCell’s energy saving state in UE database and SCell’s energy saving state in rrmEligibleScellsList are equal (see 5G_L2_16753_replaced([11154964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

If all conditions are met, then 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 [CB008898-B]For srsBfSyncIndicator equals to SyncDlSuMimo [End CB008898-B] check if any of calculated beam factor values (see 5G_L2_16753_replaced([11154964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or pdschBestBeamPowerOffsetIndex IE value, received in PsInternal_SrsBeamSelectionInd message, have changed, and proceed with next step only if values have changed [CB008898-B]. If above beam factors are not changed, but srsBfSyncIndicator equals to SyncDlSuMuMimo check also if any of these parameters: gainRatioOfNonTaperingBestToWeak, gainRatioOfTaperingToNonTapering, gainRatioOfTaperingToNonTaperingOfPairBeam value have changed, and proceed with next step only if any of values have changed [End CB008898-B],

o start or restart dedicated UE PCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

o send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to all related SCell(s) which are present in rrmEligibleScellsList according to section “Filling PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message” in 5G_L2_16748_replaced([11146924](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24IP6_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Beam data synchronization triggered by dedicated timer expiration:

[CB008898-A-UPD001]

When UE PCell timer expires (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS instance check if:

 status of CoMa aging in UE context is False (see 5G_L2_17305_replaced([11155038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242orfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If this condition is met, then 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 restart this timer, and,

 proceed with further step only for Scell(s) whose PCell’s energy saving state and SCell’s energy saving state are equal,

 send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to all related SCell(s) which are present in rrmEligibleScellsList according to section “Filling PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message” in 5G_L2_16748_replaced([11146924](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24IP6_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008898-A-UPD001]

Filling PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message:

To handle SRS BF synchronization 5G-L2-PS shall fill PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message according to below procedure:

 set modifType IE to dlSrsBmSyncNotification, then:

 if PCell’s energy saving state in UE database is equal to reducedEnergySaving or MIMO sync type from rrmEligibleScellsList equals suMimo then:

o dlSrsBmSyncParameters IE with calculated DL beam data (see 5G_L2_IF_6019_replaced([10979489](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU3_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 if PCell’s energy saving state in UE database is equal to notEnergySaving and MIMO sync type from rrmEligibleScellsList equals muMimo then:

o dlSrsBmSyncParameters IE with calculated DL beam data and with muMimoData IE (see 5G_L2_IF_6325_replaced([10979506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU4vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 if PCell’s energy saving state in UE database is equal to notEnergySaving and MIMO sync type from rrmEligibleScellsList equals taperingMuMimo IE then:

o dlSrsBmSyncParameters IE with calculated DL beam data and with muMimoData IE and taperingData IE (see 5G_L2_IF_6324_replaced([10979516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb74fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For transmission of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message when UE’s CoMa is aged (see 5G_L2_5831_replaced([11183845](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27matPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall proceed with 5G_L2_17305_replaced([11155038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242orfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.1.10.5.1.0-2 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq (ID: 11146948)

**2.1.10.5.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146963`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Handling modiftype IE equals dlSrsBmSyncNotification

Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equals to dlSrsBmSyncNotification on SCell, the SCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 check received pcellEnergySavingState IE and SCell’s energy saving state from SCell’s cell database and proceed with further steps only if the values are equal.

Otherwise, SCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall proceed according to 5G_L2_17814_replaced([11155074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_243Ps_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 check received beam data for parameters validity and proceed with further steps only if parameters are valid (see 5G_L2_16776_replaced([11155026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oq_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Otherwise, SCell’s 5G-L2-PS shall:

o fallback to the legacy CSI beamforming (see 5G_UP_ALG_17257_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and stop UE SCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

o send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncDisabled to indicate that received beams are not applied and raise dedicated warning.

 calculate DL beam pattern ID as sum of dftBeamStartPatternId (corresponding normal beam set or power saving beam set [CB008898-B] or tapering beam set[End CB008898-B], see 5G_L2_IF_4288_replaced([10969071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaoOPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with beam factor (see 5G_L2_IF_6019_replaced([10979489](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU3_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and save all received parameters, and

 start or restart dedicated UE SCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and

 response through PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to PCell with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncNotification to indicate successful beam data application.

[CB008898-B]For MU-MIMO L2-PS shall additional perform actions according to 5G_L2_19687_replaced([11155085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_243PtfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008898-B]

Handling modiftype IE equals dlSrsBmSyncDisabled

Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message (see 5G_L2_IF_656_replaced([10979441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VbU1vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncDisabled on SCell, the SCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 fallback to the legacy CSI beamforming (see 5G_UP_ALG_17257_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and stop UE SCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 send PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to PCell with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncNotification.

Handling modiftype IE equals deactivate or ohDeactivate

When SCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance receives PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq message with modifType IE equal to deactivate or ohDeactivate for UE which uses SRS synchronized beams (see 5G_L2_16750_replaced([11146948](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24IP7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the instance shall:

 fallback to the legacy CSI beamforming (see 5G_UP_ALG_17257_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and stop UE SCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 continue the legacy procedure of SCell deactivation (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_311_replaced([11195870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrYfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 2.1.10.5.1.0-3 PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp (ID: 11146971)

**2.1.10.5.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11146978`)

PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingReq Handling dlSrsBmSyncNotification

Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncNotification on PCell, the PCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance shall continue SRS DL BF synchronization (see 5G_UP_ALG_17257_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Handling dlSrsBmSyncDisabled

Upon reception of PsPeerCtrl_ScellUeSchedulingResp message (see 5G_L2_IF_658_replaced([10979530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vb75Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with modifType IE equal to dlSrsBmSyncDisabled on PCell, the PCell’s 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 remove corresponding SCell from rrmEligibleScellsList in UE context (see 5G_L2_16753_replaced([11154964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oofvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 stop UE PCell timer (see 5G_L2_16774_replaced([11155007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_242oqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only if rrmEligibleScellsList is empty. If rrmEligibleScellsList contains nrCellIdentity of other SCell, then the UE PCell timer shall not be stopped.

---

## 2.1.14 Resource Usage Procedures

### 2.1.14.0-2 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of active Ue contexts (ID: 11147062)

**2.1.14.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147072`)

Resource Usage Procedures The number of nbOfActiveUEs contexts per cellgroup is reported for UL and DL directions in the PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Once a context is allocated (for temporary or permanante context) then nbOfActiveUEs is incremented by one for each direction.

For FR1 there is one cell per cellgroup so nbOfActiveUEs context per cellgroup represents the number of UE contexts of the unique cell of the cellgroup. There is one context consumed per carrier regardless if it's Pscell or Scell.

For FR2 nbOfActiveUEs reprensents the number of UE contexts per cellgroup common to all cells for each UE.

Each time a ue context is deleted (temporary or permanante) then nbOfActiveUEs is decremented for each direction.

---

### 2.1.14.0-3 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting active UE IDs (ID: 12827835)

**2.1.14.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12827838`)

Resource Usage Procedures The list of active first 10 UE contexts IDs in DU and CU is reported to 5G-CP-RT when includeL2UeIds is set to TRUE in PsCell_GetResourceUsageReq. ueIds structure includes UE IDs from DL and UL scheduler (duplicates are merged).

---

### 2.1.14.0-4 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of temp Ue contexts (ID: 11147079)

**2.1.14.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12875025`)

Resource Usage Procedures **[Before CNI-131441] The number of temporary Ue contexts per cellgroup is reported for UL and DL directions in the PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

The definition of temporary Ue context can be found in 5G_UP_ALG_18931_replaced([11152830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksieo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Temporary Ue context is only used in the contention based RA (or msg1 corresponds to non dedicated preamble).

The number of temporary context is updated for each direction as follow:

Each time a new context is created in UL or DL the nbOfTemporaryUEs corresponding to same direction is incremented.

Once a PsUser_UserSetupReq is received (isUserSetupDone is passed to true) then the temporary context is deleted then the nbOfTemporaryUEs is decremented for each direction.

Each time a ue context is deleted and this context didn't received a ueSetup (isUserSetupDone is false) then nbOfTemporaryUEs is decremented.

note: as first step this timer is for indication only.

The number of temporary Ue Contexts will be hardcoded to 0.**[End CNI-131441]**

---

### 2.1.14.0-5 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of active SRBs and DRB bearers (ID: 11147094)

**2.1.14.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147101`)

Resource Usage Procedures number of active SRBs and active DRBs are reported respectivelly in nbOfActiveSRBs and nbOfActiveDRBs in PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see 5G_L2_IF_1673_replaced([10973201](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

At reception of PsUser_UserSetupReq nbOfActiveSRBs is incremented by numSrbs and nbOfActiveDRBs is incremented by numDrbs (see 5G_L2_IF_390_replaced([10974651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

At reception of PsUser_UserDeleteReq message nbOfActiveSRBs is decremented by number of SRBs already associated to corresponding Ue context and nbOfActiveDRBs decremented by number of DRBs already associated to corresponding Ue context .

At reception of PsUser_BearerSetupReq message nbOfActiveSRBs is incremented by numSrbs and nbOfActiveDRBs is incremented by numDrbs (see 5G_L2_IF_496_replaced([10977222](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VLdMvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

At reception of PsUser_BearerDeleteReq message nbOfActiveSRBs is decremented by number of SRBs in logicalChannelIdentity[] and nbOfActiveDRBs is decremented by number of DRBs in logicalChannelIdentity[] (see 5G_L2_IF_504_replaced([10977320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VMERPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 2.1.14.0-6 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of availiable CRNTI (ID: 11147106)

**2.1.14.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11147112`)

Resource Usage Procedures The number of availiable CRNTI (free) per cellgroup is reported in the PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

note1: for FR1 there is only one cell/cellgroup.

note2: for FR2 all cells in same cellgroup are using same crntiPoolId.

See 5G_CP_OTH_267_replaced([11597181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y23Z7PwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 2.1.14.0-7 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of Temp CRNTI (ID: 11147119)

**2.1.14.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11147125`)

Resource Usage Procedures The number of temporary CRNTIs per cellgroup is reported in the PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The desciption of temporary CRNTI generation can be found in 5G_UP_ALG_3391_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Temporary CRNTI is associated to the temporary Ue context ie it's only used in the contention based RA (or msg1 corresponds to non dedicated preamble).

Same logic will be used to increment/decrement number of temporary CRNTI as temporary Ue context see 5G_L2_4542_replaced([11147079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24JeAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

note: as first step this timer is for indication only.

---

### 2.1.14.0-8 Resource Usage Procedures Reporting of number of free timers in TimerWheels (ID: 11147133)

**2.1.14.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11147139`)

Resource Usage Procedures The number of free timers in pre-Timerwheel and post-Timerwheel respectively (pre-scheduler and post-scheduler) for DL and UL dirctions per cellgroup is reported in the PsCell_getResourceUsageResp described in 5G_L2_IF_1659_replaced([10973195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Uzpxfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

nbOfFreeTimers should contain the difference between the maxNumberOfTimerEntries and numTimersAllocated.

note: NRT SRS timer is not reported because it's in a different EO that is not managed yet by reporting resource procedure.

---

## 2.1.15 Positioning Procedures

### 2.1.15.1 Positioning cell setup

#### 2.1.15.1.0-1 Positioning cell setup Overview (ID: 11147159)

**2.1.15.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147173`)

Positioning cell setup [Before CB010680-C]Upon receiving the message, the 5G-L2-PS shall allocate a new positioning cell context identified by nrPosCellIdentity and store the parameters included in the received message into the context. [CB010680-C]

The positioning cell setup procedure is initiated through the PsPos_PosCellSetupReq and varies depending on deployment scenario:

  * When the 5G-L2-PS is in positioning dedicated cells deployment (see 5G_L2_21752), 5G_L2_21006 “Procedure in 5G-L2-PS positioning dedicated deployment” applies
  * When the 5G-L2-PS is not in positioning dedicated cells deployment, 5G_L2_21004 “Procedure in 5G-L2-PS non-positioning deployment” applies



[End CB010680-C]

---

#### 2.1.15.1.0-2 Positioning cell setup Procedure in 5G-L2-PS non-positioning deployment (ID: 11147181)

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147186`)

Positioning cell setup Reception of PsPos_PosCellSetupReq

---

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147193`)

Positioning cell setup Upon receiving the message, the 5G-L2-PS shall allocate a new positioning cell context identified by nrPosCellIdentity and store the parameters into the context. 5G-L2-PS shall respond to 5G-CP-RT as described in 5G_L2_21015.

[CB007880-A]

When PsPos_PosCellSetupReq message is received, 5G-L2-PS shall validate it according to rules described in 5G_L2_IF_6754_replaced([10982231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VwE_fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_IF_6756_replaced([10982256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VwsAfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the validation passes, 5G-L2-PS shall perform positioning cell setup procedure containing following steps:

1\. Assign the positioning cell to the Positioning Scheduler (see 5G_L2_22661)

2\. Perform positioning cell context setup (see 5G_L2_22662)

3\. Send response to 5G-CP-RT (see 5G_L2_21015)

If the validation fails, 5G-L2-PS shall send not ok response to 5G-CP-RT (see 5G_L2_21015).

Procedure shall be guarded with timer, see 5G_L2_21017.

[End CB007880-A]

---

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11147199`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell assignment to positioning scheduler

---

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147206`)

Positioning cell setup According to received l2SubpoolId, firstCellSlotId 5G-L2-PS shall assign the positioning cell to positioning scheduler mapping into its schIndex on the core rules as defined in 5G_L2_4307 when EO startup

---

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11147211`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell context setup

---

**2.1.15.1.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147217`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall create a new positioning cell context identified by PsPos_PosCellSetupReq.nrPosCellIdentity IE and store the parameters included in the received message.

---

#### 2.1.15.1.0-3 Positioning cell setup Procedure in 5G-L2-PS positioning dedicated deployment (ID: 11147223)

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147228`)

Positioning cell setup Reception of PsPos_PosCellSetupReq

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147237`)

Positioning cell setup When PsPos_PosCellSetupReq message is received, 5G-L2-PS shall validate it according to rules described in 5G_L2_IF_6754_replaced([10982231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VwE_fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_IF_6756_replaced([10982256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VwsAfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the validation passes, 5G-L2-PS shall perform positioning cell setup procedure containing following steps:

1\. Assign the positioning cell to the Positioning Scheduler (see 5G_L2_22078)

2\. Perform positioning subcell uplink addressing procedure (see 5G_L2_21011, 5G_L2_21013)

[CB010680-G]

3\. Establish slot synchronization for Positioning Scheduler (see 5G_L2_23242)

[End CB010680-G]

4\. Perform positioning cell context setup (see 5G_L2_21009)

5\. Send response to 5G-CP-RT (see 5G_L2_21015)

If the validation fails, 5G-L2-PS shall send not ok response to 5G-CP-RT (see 5G_L2_21015).

Procedure shall be guarded with timer, see 5G_L2_21017.

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11147244`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell assignment to positioning scheduler

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147251`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall assign the positioning cell to positioning scheduler according to received l2SubpoolId, firstCellSlotId and deployment rules as described in 5G_L2_4307 and 5G_L2_21752.

5G-L2-PS shall comply with the L2Subpool cell slot framework (see 5G_UP_3551_replaced([11387082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufEqjfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_7378_replaced([11390296](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufSF8fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for positioning cells, following the same approach as it is done for nrCellGrps. For that purpose 5G-L2-PS shall use PsPos_PosCellSetupReq.numCellSlots parameter to validate if there is enough capacity left in given L2Subpool.

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11147258`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell context setup

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147264`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall create a new positioning cell context identified by PsPos_PosCellSetupReq.nrPosCellIdentity IE and store the parameters included in the received message.

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11147271`)

Positioning cell setup Transmission of UlData_AddressReq for positioning subcell

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11147275`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall build and send UlData_AddressReq to 5G-L1-UL with parameters:

  * subcellId set to PsPos_PosCellSetupReq.ulPosSubcellList.posSubcellId (ulPosSubcellList shall contain only one element according to 5G_L2_IF_6754_replaced([10982231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VwE_fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) validation)
  * prachReceiveIndAddress set to 0xFFFFFFFF (prachReceiveIndAddress is not used in positioning subcell)
  * diagnosticIndAddress set to Positioning Scheduler (PosSch) L1 communication address

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11147283`)

Positioning cell setup Reception of UlData_AddressResp for positioning subcell

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147291`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall handle the UlData_AddressResp send by 5G-L1-UL. If the status IE equals NOK, 5G-L2-PS shall respond with the PsPos_PosCellSetupResp with not ok status, see 5G_L2_21015.

Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall store the srsPosReceiveReqAddress IE. Other IEs can be discarded as they are not used for positioning subcell.

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11147297`)

Positioning cell setup Slot synchronization for Positioning Scheduler establishment

---

**2.1.15.1.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11147305`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall initialize and maintain NR-slot-based synchronization for the positioning cell in the positioning scheduler using the Aa5GTimerCreateWithEvent(_) platform API function, using parameters provided in the PsPos_PosCellSetupReq: oneWayHwDelayDl, frameStartSub10ms, frameStartSFN, tddFrameStructure.referenceScs. The Aa5GTimerCreateWithEvent(_) function shall be called with arguments calculated following the 5G_L1L2_FLOW_672_replaced([11177470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeTrwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) diagram, excluding 5G-L2-LO related part. The 10 SFN synchronization shift should be also excluded, however 5G-L2-PS shall keep some shift (i.e. one NR slot) to guarantee the Aa5GTimerCreateWithEvent(*) is called with future reference time.

---

#### 2.1.15.1.0-4 Positioning cell setup Transmission of PsPos_PosCellSetupResp (ID: 11147311)

**2.1.15.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11147317`)

Positioning cell setup 5G-L2-PS shall send the PsPos_PosCellSetupResp in Positioning cell setup procedure (successful or unsuccessful). Depending on the outcome the IEs shall be filled:

  * messageResult.status: see 5G_UP_1846_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
  * messageResult.cause: see 5G_UP_1846_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
  * nrPosCellIdentity set to PsPos_PosCellSetupReq.nrPosCellIdentity,
  * needForRollback set to TRUE, if the procedure was unsuccessful and any internal context was already set up,
  * [Before CB010680-G] diagnosticInformation not set (Rationale: For positioning cells, no additional diagnostic information is required from 5G-L2-PS by other components) [End CB010680-G]

---

#### 2.1.15.1.0-5 Positioning cell setup Procedure guard timer (ID: 11147325)

**2.1.15.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147331`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell setup timer management

---

**2.1.15.1.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147337`)

Positioning cell setup Timer shall be started upon receiving PsPos_PosCellSetupReq with the value of rdL1L2CellSetupProcedureTimer (see 5G_L2_15079).

Timer shall be stopped when sending PsPos_PosCellSetupResp.

---

**2.1.15.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11147346`)

Positioning cell setup Positioning cell setup timer timeout

---

**2.1.15.1.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147352`)

Positioning cell setup When 5G-L2-PS detects the timeout of timer started as described in 5G_L2_21018, 5G-L2-PS shall interrupt the Positioning cell setup procedure and respond with PsPos_PosCellSetupResp with the following IEs:

\- status set to EStatus5G_NotOk,

\- the cause is set to 0x00000009 (ECause5G_ProcedureTimeOut 5G_UP_1846_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

\- needForRollback set to TRUE

---

### 2.1.15.2 Positioning cell delete

#### 2.1.15.2.1 Reception of PsPos_PosCellDeleteReq

##### 2.1.15.2.1.0-1 Reception of PsPos_PosCellDeleteReq Overview (ID: 11147372)

**2.1.15.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147387`)

Reception of PsPos_PosCellDeleteReq Upon receiving the message, the 5G-L2-PS shall:

  * remove positioning cell context identified by nrPosCellIdentity



[CB010680-G]

  * remove this positioning cell from the related measurement contexts (see Measurement setup 5G_L2_IF_6503_replaced([10982437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vx6IPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



[End CB010680-G]

5G-L2-PS shall respond to 5G-CP-RT with PsPos_PosCellDeleteResp with nrPosCellIdentity set to value received in request message.

---

### 2.1.15.3 Measurement setup

#### 2.1.15.3.1 Reception of PsPos_MeasSetupReq

##### 2.1.15.3.1.0-1 Reception of PsPos_MeasSetupReq Overview (ID: 11147408)

**2.1.15.3.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147421`)

Reception of PsPos_MeasSetupReq Upon receiving the message, 5G-L2-PS should allocate a new measurement context, and store the parameters included in the received message into the context.

[CB007880-A] L2PS shall respond by PsPos_MeasSetupResp of the message. Refer to 5G_L2_IF_6503_replaced([10982437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Vx6IPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB007880-A]

5G-L2-PS shall start to schedule srs resource configured in the received message.

---

### 2.1.15.4 Measurement update

#### 2.1.15.4.1 Reception of PsPos_MeasUpdateReq

##### 2.1.15.4.1.0-1 Reception of PsPos_MeasUpdateReq Overview (ID: 11147440)

**2.1.15.4.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147447`)

Reception of PsPos_MeasUpdateReq Upon receiving the message, L2PS should find the measurement context identified by "ranMeasId" in received message, update the context with parameters received.

If a parameter already stored in the context, it shall be set by the value included in received message. If an optional parameter structure is not stored in the received message, the earlier received values of the parameter shall not be changed.

If srs resource configuration included in received message, 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling srs resource earlier configured and start to schedule srs resource included in the received message.

---

### 2.1.15.5 Measurement abort

#### 2.1.15.5.1 Reception of PsPos_MeasAbortReq

##### 2.1.15.5.1.0-1 Reception of PsPos_MeasAbortReq Overview (ID: 11147466)

**2.1.15.5.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147471`)

Reception of PsPos_MeasAbortReq Upon receiving the message, L2PS should stop scheduling for srs resource configured and remove the measurement context identified by "ranMeasId" included in received message.

---
